#+END_VERSE


* 484. Tomorrow's supreme surprise

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:484
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Yesterday's supreme surprise:
Today I shall realise God.

Today's supreme surprise:
Tomorrow I shall become another God.

Tomorrow's supreme surprise:
The day after tomorrow I shall resign
And give back to my predecessor
His post,
His responsibility,
His headache.

#+END_VERSE


* 485. Totally lost

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:485
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

When an iota of faith is lost
A God-seeker is totally lost.

When a fraction of courage is lost
A God-warrior is totally lost.

When a particle of life is lost
A God-dreamer is totally lost.

#+END_VERSE


* 486. We do not dare

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:486
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

You do not dare to know
The real truth.

He does not dare to face
The real light.

I do not dare to attain
The real silence.

#+END_VERSE


* 487. Inventions

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:487
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Doubt
Is earth-invention.

Faith
Is Heaven-invention.

Compassion
Is God-invention.

Suspicion
Is man-invention.

Satisfaction
Is love-invention.

#+END_VERSE


* 488. Life is like love

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:488
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Life is like love;
It adores their common source:
Delight.

Truth is like love and life;
It invokes their common Goal:
Perfection.

#+END_VERSE


* 489. My hope is a greedy fellow

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:489
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

My hope is a subtle, greedy fellow.
I shall not like him
Any more.

My inner cry is an unnoticed, working fellow.
I shall start loving him dearly
Right from today.

#+END_VERSE


* 490. A lost connection

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:490
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

My Father, God, invited me
When He celebrated
The first morning
Of my younger brother, Time.
Alas, since then I have kept
No connection with
Either my Father or my brother.
Alas, I do hope
That they will give me
Their forgiveness-light,
Their forgetfulness-night.

#+END_VERSE


* 491. Earth-king, Heaven-king

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:491
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Laughter is earth-king
When I live in the soul.

Terror is earth-king
When I live in the body.

Satisfaction is Heaven-king
When I live in the soul.

Imagination is Heaven-king
When I live in the body.

#+END_VERSE


* 492. All are unhappy

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:492
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

You are unhappy
That you are not God.

He is unhappy
That he is not a divine man.

I am unhappy
That still I do not have
The necessary capacity
To escape the embrace
Of the animal-kingdom.

#+END_VERSE


* 493. Man revolts

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:493
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Man revolts
Against the higher Will
Because
Man has discovered a voice.

The higher will does not revolt
Against man's voice
Because
It always likes to work
In accordance with God's Choice.

#+END_VERSE


* 494. God-Beauty

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:494
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Earth-beauty
Increases his impurity.

Heaven-beauty
Increases his purity.

God-Beauty
Transforms his impurity
Into purity's flood.

God-Beauty
Transforms his purity
Into Immortality's Sea.

#+END_VERSE


* 495. God stays with me

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:495
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

To be one with my sadness
God stays with me,
Inside my earth-role.

To be one with my gladness
God stays with me,
Inside my Heaven-soul.

#+END_VERSE


* 496. Arrows of the sun

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:496
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

The arrows of the outer sun
Kill my long-cherished
Earth-pride.

The arrows of the inner sun
Open my long-forgotten
Heaven-door.

#+END_VERSE


* 497. My body and my life

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:497
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Since God loves me now,
I shall definitely love myself,
My body and my life.
I shall no more hate myself,
My body and my life.

Since God uses me now,
I shall definitely use myself,
My body and my life.
I shall no more keep unemployed myself,
My body and my life.

#+END_VERSE


* 498. My soul climbs down

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:498
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

My soul climbs down with Heaven
To celebrate Heaven's first few days
On earth.

My heart climbs up with earth
To celebrate earth's first few days
In Heaven,
And to protect it from getting lost
In the sun-brilliance up there.

#+END_VERSE


* 499. God gave me what I needed

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:499
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Realisation I needed.
God gave it to me openly.

Perfection I needed.
God gave it to me secretly.

Satisfaction I needed.
God gave it to me slowly,
Steadily
And
Unconditionally.

#+END_VERSE


* 500. My God-realisation

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:500
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

My God-realisation
Was my Olympian joy.

My God-revelation
Is my Herculean duty.

My God-manifestation
Shall be my Himalayan peace.

#+END_VERSE


* Part VI -- poems 501 to 600[fn:: EB 501-600. Poems 501 to 600 were written in Zurich and Geneva, Switzerland.]

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: section
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:501e1
  :END:




* 501. Sweet trance

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:501
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

When I pray
I enter into my heart's
Sweet trance.

When I meditate
I enter into my life's
Sweet trance.

When I love
I enter into my God's
Sweet trance.

#+END_VERSE


* 502. Lean upon me

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:502
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Lean upon my heart.
I shall give you
What I have and what I am:
Aspiration-drop.

Lean upon my soul.
I shall give you
What God has and what God is:
Compassion-sea.

#+END_VERSE


* 503. Death-discoveries

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:503
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

His body's discovery:
Death is a ruthless finisher.

His heart's discovery:
Death is a bountiful awakener.

His soul's discovery:
Death is a sincere life-seeker.

#+END_VERSE


* 504. Your heart

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:504
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

You have a truth-aspiring heart;
Therefore
I love you deeply.

You have a love-offering heart;
Therefore
I adore you immensely.

You have a God-surrendering heart;
Therefore
I need you eternally.

#+END_VERSE


* 505. Here is my life-car

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:505
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Mind, here is my life-car.
Be careful,
Since you are only a beginner.
Be careful,
Don't run into an accident.

Heart, here is my life-car.
Be cheerful;
Drive as fast as you can,
Since you are an excellent driver.
Be cheerful;
Today the Lord Supreme shall watch you driving.

#+END_VERSE


* 506. Space, height, depth

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:506
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Falsehood-existence
Is a known space.

Truth-existence
Is an unknown height.

Love-existence
Is an unknowable depth.

#+END_VERSE


* 507. Heart-light, body-night

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:507
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

I am all fear
When I see my body-night
Behind my heart-light.
My body-night can easily
Capture me and devour me
If I fail to run with my heart-light.

I have no fear
When I see my heart-light
Behind my body-night.
I tell my body-night that
Since I am a slow runner
I shall run only with my heart-light,
And I flatter my body-night
Into maintaining its own speed.
Thus, I save myself
With my heart-light.

#+END_VERSE


* 508. My strength

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:508
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Life is my strength,
Love is my strength,
Silence is my strength.
My life-strength I use
To fight against death.
My love-strength I use
To awaken humanity.
My silence-strength I use
To feed divinity.

#+END_VERSE


* 509. Don't mix with him

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:509
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

For God's sake, don't mix with him.
He has a heavy load
Of worldly pride.
He may ask you to share his burden.

For my sake, don't mix with him.
He is a heavy load
Of heavenly failure.
His very presence is extremely poisonous
And terribly dangerous.

#+END_VERSE


* 510. At the end of my journey

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:510
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

At the end
Of my journey's length,
Whom shall I see?
My Beloved Supreme.
What shall I see?
His Smile.

At the end
Of my journey's depth,
Whom shall I see?
My Beloved Supreme.
What shall I receive?
His Blessing.

At the end
Of my journey's height,
Whom shall I see?
My Beloved Supreme.
What shall I become?
His, unconditionally His.

#+END_VERSE


* 511. I treasure

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:511
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

A sweet and divine heart of prayer
I treasure openly.

A pure and supreme heart of meditation
I treasure secretly.

A perfect and absolute life of God
I treasure sleeplessly.

#+END_VERSE


* 512. The fount

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:512
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

What is the fount of my life?
Delight.

What is the fount of my love?
Delight.

What is the fount of my perfection?
Delight.

What is the fount of my God?
Silence.

#+END_VERSE


* 513. Faith

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:513
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

The flames of faith
I need
To walk along
The outer road.

The sun of faith
I need
To run the length of
The inner road.

#+END_VERSE


* 514. Yet he lives

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:514
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

His rainbow-beauty life has faded.
Yet he lives.

His moon-beauty life has disappeared.
Yet he lives.

His sun-beauty life has failed.
Yet he lives.

#+END_VERSE


* 515. Heaven-born music

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:515
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Earth-born music
Nobody needs;
No, not even my stupid mind.

Heaven-born music
Everybody needs,
Including my wise soul.

#+END_VERSE


* 516. Yet I love him

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:516
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

His wicked eyes
Know my weaknesses.
His wicked heart
Has tested my strength.
His wicked life
Has destroyed my joy.
Yet I love him.
Why?
Because he loves me
As his own, very own.

#+END_VERSE


* 517. The dream of Bliss

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:517
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

The dream of Bliss
God and I
Together enjoy
In the heart of God's Silence-height.

The Bliss of dream
My heart and I
Together enjoy
In the life of earth's sound-flight.

#+END_VERSE


* 518. Too weak to move

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:518
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Too weak to move,
Yet I smilingly move
To give Heaven my place to sit.

Too strong to move,
Yet I unconditionally move
To give earth my place to sit.

#+END_VERSE


* 519. The darlings of earth and Heaven

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:519
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Two are the darlings of earth:
My hope-life
And
My despair heart.

Two are the darlings of Heaven:
My aspiration-cry
And
My surrender-smile.

#+END_VERSE


* 520. Earth-voice, Heaven-choice

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:520
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

His earth-voice
Was not meant
For Heaven-music.

His Heaven-choice
Was not meant
For earth-singers.

#+END_VERSE


* 521. My family

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:521
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Body,
You are too impure to touch.

Vital,
You are too wild to tame.

Mind,
You are too mean to see.

Heart,
You are too weak to love.

Soul,
You are too pure to be.

#+END_VERSE


* 522. Each surrender-smile

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:522
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Each thought-power
Is national.

Each will-light
Is international.

Each surrender-smile
Is eternally liberal.

#+END_VERSE


* 523. My form

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:523
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

When my form resolves,
God smiles with joy.

When my form dissolves,
God weeps with pride.

#+END_VERSE


* 524. Lustre

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:524
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Lustre-aspiration,
Indeed, you are your Lord's Eternity's Grace.

Lustre-surrender,
Indeed, you are your Lord's Eternity's Treasure.

#+END_VERSE


* 525. Affairs

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:525
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Earth-affairs
I do not want to know
Because
They are too silly for me.

Heaven-affairs
I do not want to know
Because
They are too high for me.

God-affairs
I know and always shall know
Because
They are very dear to me.

#+END_VERSE


* 526. Time and becoming

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:526
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Earth-time
Tells me what I cannot become:
A real man.

Heaven-time
Tells me what I can become:
A real God.

God-time
Tells me what I have already become:
God's perfection-seeker,
God's satisfaction-lover.

#+END_VERSE


* 527. Stoop and conquer

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:527
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Your strength stoops
Because
You love your body's countless demands,
Not unconsciously but consciously.

Your strength conquers
Because
You listen to your soul's whispering voice,
Not unconsciously but unconditionally.

#+END_VERSE


* 528. Gifts from my heritage

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:528
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

From my Heaven-heritage
I have received
God-smile
And
God-satisfaction.

From my earth-heritage
I have received
God-cry
And
God-compassion.

#+END_VERSE


* 529. Waiting for God's Hour

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:529
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

The beggar-seeker in me
Knows not how to wait
For God's Hour.

The emperor-lover in me
Not only knows how to wait,
But has been waiting
For God's Hour
Cheerfully
And
Unconditionally.

#+END_VERSE


* 530. Birthday expectations

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:530
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

I expect nothing
From the birthday
Of my earth-body
Because
My earth-body
Is my frustration-sea.

I expect everything
From the birthday
Of my Heaven-soul
Because
My Heaven-soul
Is God's God-promise to me,
God's God-satisfaction in me.

#+END_VERSE


* 531. They came to me

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:531
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Beauty came to me
Like the morning rose.

Duty came to me
Like the morning sun.

Divinity came to me
Like the morning aspiration.

#+END_VERSE


* 532. I shall pour into thee

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:532
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

My soul,
I shall gladly pour into thee
What I have:
Aspiration-flames.

My heart,
I shall devotedly pour into thee
What I am:
Failure-night.

#+END_VERSE


* 533. Heaven's day, earth's night

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:533
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

I shall make
My Heaven's day long
So that I can receive
More Light, abundant Light,
From God.

I shall make
My earth's night empty
So that I can fill it with
God-light
And
God-perfection.

#+END_VERSE


* 534. Then and now

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:534
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

A heart that aspired soulfully
I had.
A life that dedicated divinely
I had.
Alas, but now I have a heart
Afraid of aspiration,
Now I have a life
Afraid of dedication.

#+END_VERSE


* 535. His love of beauty

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:535
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

God-Beauty
He loves occasionally.

Heaven-beauty
He loves unmindfully.

Earth-beauty
He loves secretly.

His beauty
He loves
Shamelessly,
Breathlessly.

#+END_VERSE


* 536. Duty

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:536
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

A good thought
Is a serving duty.

A strong will
Is a fulfilling duty.

A divine surrender
Is an unparalleled duty.

#+END_VERSE


* 537. I love my days and nights

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:537
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

I love my days
Because
They reveal God-dance.

I love my nights
Because
They manifest God-trance.

#+END_VERSE


* 538. Surrendering dedication

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:538
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Damaging imperfection:
That is what I was.

Crying expectation:
That is what I am.

Surrendering dedication:
That is what I shall be.

#+END_VERSE


* 539. Life, love and service

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:539
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

My life
Is the bow of my Lord Supreme.

My love
Is the flow of my Lord Supreme.

My service
Is the glow of my Lord Supreme.

#+END_VERSE


* 540. Three songs

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:540
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

A Heavenly song
Inspired me to strive and become.

An earthly song
Instigated me to deceive and achieve.

A God-song
Liberated me to divinise and immortalise
Earth-cry
And
Earth-surrender.

#+END_VERSE


* 541. Beauty's eloquence

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:541
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Beauty's eloquence
I appreciate.

Beauty's silence
I admire.

Beauty's presence
My world desires.

#+END_VERSE


* 542. I feel so sorry

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:542
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

My Heaven-life,
I feel so sorry
That earth-soul
Does not care for you.

My earth-soul,
I feel so sorry
That Heaven-goal
Has no need for you.

#+END_VERSE


* 543. What can you do?

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:543
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Heaven is deaf.
What can you do,
Poor earth?

Earth is blind.
What can you do,
Poor Heaven?

I am unbearable.
What can You do,
Poor God?

#+END_VERSE


* 544. Sweet were the days

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:544
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Brave were the days
When I fought for God
And succeeded.
Sweet were the days
When God
In me and through me
Proceeded.

#+END_VERSE


* 545. What you are to me

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:545
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Father: Compassion-Perfection,
This is what You are to me.

"Daughter: Satisfaction-dedication,
This is what you are to Me."

#+END_VERSE


* 546. My teachers

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:546
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Birth teaches me
How to aspire,
Why to aspire.

Death teaches me
How to rest,
When to rest.

God teaches me
How to surrender,
How to become.

#+END_VERSE


* 547. My ways

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:547
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Secret are my ways
When I am one with earth aspiration.

Sacred are my ways
When I am one with Heaven-illumination.

Sincere are my ways
When I am one with God-Compassion.

#+END_VERSE


* 548. My life-realisation

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:548
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Death is sweet,
Life is sweeter,
Truth is sweetest,
Love-oneness is sweeter than the sweetest:
That is my life-realisation.

#+END_VERSE


* 549. Because they help him

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:549
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Why does he love his enemies?
Because
They help him unconsciously
In his heart-expansion.

Why does he love his friends?
Because
They help him consciously
In his life-satisfaction.

Why does he love God?
Because
God helps him unconditionally
In his God-realisation.

#+END_VERSE


* 550. Beggars

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:550
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Hope is a beggar;
It needs earth wealth.

Earth-wealth is a beggar;
It needs perfection-health.

Perfection-health is a beggar;
It needs realisation-satisfaction.

#+END_VERSE


* 551. The inner sun

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:551
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

The rainbow comes and goes
With a charming body.
The outer sun comes and goes
With a vast body.
The inner sun stays and stays
With its boundless
And deathless
Love-light.

#+END_VERSE


* 552. I cannot say

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:552
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

I cannot say
Who I was.

I cannot say
Where I was.

I cannot say
What I was
But
I unmistakably know
What I shall be:
I shall be God's God-Height.

#+END_VERSE


* 553. I dare

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:553
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

I dare to cry;
Therefore
The Divinity above loves me.

I dare to smile;
Therefore
The humanity in me loves me.

I dare to become;
Therefore
The Immortality before me claims me.

#+END_VERSE


* 554. O Eternity's sunrise

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:554
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

O Eternity's sunrise,
How far shall you
Succeed and proceed in me?

O Eternity's sunset,
Why have I failed?
Why? Why?

#+END_VERSE


* 555. Born again

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:555
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

My desire-life is crying
Because
Death is born again.

My aspiration-life is dancing
Because
A living God is born again.

#+END_VERSE


* 556. Somewhere I saw God

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:556
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Somewhere far beyond my mind
I saw God's Body.
Somewhere within my heart
I saw God's Face.
Somewhere inside my soul
I saw God's Smile.
And now I see
God-perfection
Inside my surrender-home.

#+END_VERSE


* 557. His life thunders and whispers

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:557
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

His vital does not aspire,
His mind does not aspire;
Therefore
His life thunders in dreams.

His heart aspires,
His soul aspires;
Therefore
His life whispers in realities.

#+END_VERSE


* 558. Smile a little more

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:558
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Father, smile a little more
In my heart.
"Daughter, cry a little more
In My Heart."

Father, I am sorry;
My heart tears are sleeping.
"Daughter, I am sorry;
My Soul-tears are not functioning."

#+END_VERSE


* 559. Mutual discoveries

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:559
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Some fools have discovered
In him
Their most precious idol.
He has discovered
In them
His most perfect doll.
Poor God has surrendered
To their brooding
Ignorance-night.

#+END_VERSE


* 560. Believe in his realisation!

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:560
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Some fools do not believe
In his God-realisation.
He has forgiven their
Imperfect vision.
But God says to them:
You fools,
Believe in his realisation!
If not, you are doomed
To live in futile imagination.

#+END_VERSE


* 561. God laughs at my stupidity

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:561
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

When I use
The wings of an angel,
God laughs at my stupidity.

When I use
The wings of the stars,
God laughs at my stupidity.

When I use
The wings of the moon,
God laughs at my stupidity.

But when I use
My two human feet,
God prides Himself
On my sagacity.

#+END_VERSE


* 562. When I live in the soul

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:562
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

When I live in the mind,
I soar from the unknown
To the unknown.

When I live in the heart,
I soar from the known
To the known.

When I live in the soul,
I soar from the ever-known
To the ever-known.

#+END_VERSE


* 563. Can't you surrender?

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:563
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

O mind of man,
Do not sleep anymore.
Can't you hear God
Knocking and knocking
At your door?

O heart of man,
Can't you surrender
Your insecurity-drop
To God-Ocean
And
Become the ocean-soul,
Ocean-body
And God-satisfaction?

#+END_VERSE


* 564. God's Compassion

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:564
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

God's Compassion
Has awakened my body's sleep.

God's Concern
Has sweetened my vital's madness.

God's Concentration
Has illumined my mind's blindness.

God's Satisfaction
Has immortalised my heart's selflessness.

#+END_VERSE


* 565. Their qualifications

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:565
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

My body knows
How to cry.
That is its qualification.

My vital knows
How to bind.
That is its qualification.

My mind knows
How to blind.
That is its qualification.

My heart knows
How to climb.
That is its qualification.

#+END_VERSE


* 566. Shall I ever?

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:566
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

I am waiting
For a new dawn.
Alas, shall I ever see a new dawn?

I am looking
For an old friend.
Alas, shall I ever find an old friend?

I am crying
For the eternal Silence.
Alas, shall I ever glimpse the eternal Silence?

#+END_VERSE


* 567. The power of his beauty

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:567
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

The power of his beauty
Lights me
But
Never warms me.
The beauty of his power
Not only warms me,
But also illumines me,
Liberates me
And
Immortalises me.

#+END_VERSE


* 568. Conceals and reveals

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:568
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Night conceals;
Morning reveals.
Night conceals
Your ignorance-life;
Morning reveals
Your aspiration-heart.

#+END_VERSE


* 569. Swimmers in the sea of peace

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:569
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

When I was
A river of thought,
I cried to flow
Into the sea of Peace.
Fruitless were my cries.
But now my surrender-life
Swims in the sea of Peace
Together with three other swimmers:
God the Compassion-swimmer,
God the Perfection-swimmer,
God the Satisfaction-swimmer.

#+END_VERSE


* 570. There was a time

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:570
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

There was a time
When I loved desire-ground.

There was a time
When I loved aspiration-hill.

There was a time
When I loved realisation-mountain.

Now I love only one thing:
God-surrender.

#+END_VERSE


* 571. All need You

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:571
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

O gracious God,
My heart needs You
Eternally.

O glorious God,
My mind needs You
Badly.

O precious God,
My life needs You
Throbbingly.

#+END_VERSE


* 572. Friends of mine

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:572
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

You are a celestial friend of mine;
Therefore
I need your smile,
You need my love.

You are a celestial friend of mine;
Therefore
I do not need your impurity,
You do not need my stupidity.

#+END_VERSE


* 573. I love God

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:573
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

I love God
Not because I always need Him.
I love God
Not because He compassionately needs me.
I love God
Because He alone knows
That I am another God.

#+END_VERSE


* 574. I shall keep God ready for you

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:574
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Young man, you may not need
God today,
But I shall keep God ready
For you
Tomorrow
In case you need Him then.

Young man, you may not love
God today,
But I shall keep God ready
For you
Tomorrow
In case you want to love Him then.

#+END_VERSE


* 575. My two lives

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:575
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

My stupidity-life
Makes me angry, animal-angry.
My sincerity-life
Makes me hungry, God-hungry.

#+END_VERSE


* 576. Aspiration neglected

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:576
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Aspiration neglected,
God-Love rejected,
Man-love suspected,
Heaven-love interrogated,
Earth-love inspected.

#+END_VERSE


* 577. Free of charge

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:577
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Too tired to think!
God, You can use my mind
From now on
Free of charge.

Too disheartened to love!
God, You can use my heart
From now on
Free of charge.

#+END_VERSE


* 578. Miniatures

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:578
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

A miniature lie:
I think of God all the time.
A miniature truth:
I have given God my realisation-height.

#+END_VERSE


* 579. She is all for God

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:579
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

She is all for God-Joy
In the morning.
She is all for God-Joy.

She is all for God-Power
At noon.
She is all for God-Power.

She is all for God-Peace
In the evening.
She is all for God-Peace.

#+END_VERSE


* 580. Dreams

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:580
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Sweet is a child's dream.
I love him and his dream.

Futile is a man's dream.
I pity him and his dream.

Real is God's Dream.
I adore God and His Dream.

#+END_VERSE


* 581. To steer humanity and divinity

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:581
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

To steer humanity
I need God's Reality-boat.
Ah, where is it?
Where is it?

To steer divinity
I need God's Dream-boat.
Ah, it has been waiting for us
For such a long time.

#+END_VERSE


* 582. She

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:582
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Her soul-greatness illumines us,
Her heart-kindness awakens us,
Her mind-alertness cautions us,
Her vital-quickness inspires us,
Her body-selflessness feeds us.

#+END_VERSE


* 583. O sweet delight

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:583
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

O sweet delight,
I feel you
Because
I am not the body.

O sweet delight,
I use you
Because
I am the truth-ordained
God-server.

#+END_VERSE


* 584. Dislikes

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:584
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

I dislike
A fault-finding eye.

I dislike
A fault-hiding mind.

I dislike
A fault-fearing heart.

#+END_VERSE


* 585. The real doer

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:585
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

I condemn no one
Because
I know no person is the real doer.
God is the real doer.

I console no one
Because
I know no person is the real sufferer.
God is the real sufferer.

#+END_VERSE


* 586. A perfect gentleman

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:586
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

I sleep at night;
Therefore
God does not disturb my sleep.
Who else could be such a perfect gentleman?

I work during the day;
Therefore
God does not disturb my work.
Who else could be such a perfect gentleman?

If I meditate anytime,
Only then will God come and converse with me.
He does not come unwanted.
He is a perfect gentleman, after all.

#+END_VERSE


* 587. Do me a favour

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:587
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Sweet Lord,
Please do me a favour.
Please steal my heart's sorrow.

Sweet Lord,
Please do me a favour.
Please steal my mind's suspicion.

Sweet Lord,
Please do me a favour.
Please steal my vital's audacity.

Sweet Lord,
Please do me a favour.
Please steal my body's timidity.

#+END_VERSE


* 588. My heart's family

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:588
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

My heart's best brother:
God-determination.

My heart's best sister:
God-dedication.

My heart's best Father:
God-liberation.

My heart's best Mother:
God-perfection.

#+END_VERSE


* 589. I enjoy his heart's hospitality

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:589
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

I enjoy
The pure hospitality
Of his heart.

I fear
The sheer curiosity
Of his mind.

I avoid
The wild vitality
Of his vital.

I dislike
The dark impurity
Of his body.

#+END_VERSE


* 590. Tell them not to depart

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:590
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Tell your mind
Not to depart
From simplicity.
Simplicity is God-Beauty.

Tell your heart
Not to depart
From sincerity.
Sincerity is God-Necessity.

#+END_VERSE


* 591. You are my peerless discovery

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:591
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

I have no power to tell you
How great your mind is
In God's Eyes.

I have no power to tell you
How good your heart is
In God's Eyes.

I have no power to tell you
How meaningful and fruitful
Your soul is
In God's Eyes.

Needless to say, you are
My peerless discovery.

#+END_VERSE


* 592. My true helpers

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:592
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

My innocent eyes
Helped me to see God's Feet.

My innocent heart
Helped me to feel God's Heart.

My innocent life
Helped me to become God's Smile.

#+END_VERSE


* 593. Innocently done

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:593
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Innocently done:
I have not loved God.
Innocently done:
I have not thought of God.
Innocently done:
I have not pleased God,
Manifested God
And
Fulfilled God.

#+END_VERSE


* 594. Sometimes useful

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:594
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Exertion is useful
When the vital is lethargic.

Severity is useful
When the mind is dogmatic.

Threat is useful
When the heart is delaying.

#+END_VERSE


* 595. Forget me not

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:595
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

A few fleeting years
Can take me
To the animal kingdom.
O Lord Supreme,
Save me, save me!

A few slow years
Can take me
To Love-Oneness-Perfection Kingdom.
O Lord Supreme,
Forget me not!
Forget me not!

#+END_VERSE


* 596. Their joy

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:596
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

His fruitful smile
Is his mother's joy.

His soulful cry
Is his father's joy.

His self-giving heart
Is God's Transcendental Joy.

#+END_VERSE


* 597. I live there no longer

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:597
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

To discover my aspiration
I live no longer
In my mind-cave.

To discover my realisation
I live no longer
In my vital-den.

To discover my perfection
I live no longer
In my body-hole.

#+END_VERSE


* 598. Originality and creativity

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:598
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

What is originality?
A new God in preparation.
What is creativity?
A new man of God-Compassion.

#+END_VERSE


* 599. His mind-heart-soul

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:599
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

His mind is nothing
But a self-styled fertile counsel.
His heart is nothing
But a sea of ceaseless cries and sighs.
His soul is nothing
But the Smile of God's Reality Dream.

#+END_VERSE


* 600. O solitude

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:600
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

O solitude,
Your God lives in a tiny
Himalayan cave;
My God lives on the top
Of the Himalayas.

O solitude,
You want me to come to you
To see the Face of God.
But I tell you
My God has already come to me
To be served and fed by me
In the sound-life of His creation-body.

#+END_VERSE


* Part VII -- poems 601 to 700[fn:: EB 601-700. Poems 601 to 700 were written in Geneva, Switzerland and Stockholm, Sweden.]

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: section
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:601e1
  :END:






* 601. Who are you?

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:601
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Who are you?
An untransformed man.

Who are you?
Earth's hope-tree
And
Heaven's dream-moon.

Who are you?
An unmanifested God.

#+END_VERSE


* 602. Give and receive

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:602
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

You shall give,
Always give.

I shall receive,
Always receive.

Indeed, I shall be grateful to you
For your supreme gifts:
God-aspiration
And
God-realisation.

#+END_VERSE


* 603. I have given you

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:603
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

I have given you,
Already given you,
And
I am ready to give you even more,
In case you need more,
My dear friend.
Strangely enough,
You have never shown
Any sign of gratitude
For my God-manifestation,
God-perfection
Gifts.

#+END_VERSE


* 604. Ignorance

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:604
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Simple ignorance:
I am for myself.
Complex ignorance:
I am of ignorance-night.
Treacherous and dangerous ignorance:
God is not for me.

#+END_VERSE


* 605. Are we not even?

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:605
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

The sweet bonds of remembrance:
You gave me, Lord,
Your supreme Treasure:
Compassion.
I gave You, Lord,
My supreme treasure:
Surrender.
Are we not even?
"Certainly we are, My child."

#+END_VERSE


* 606. She blossomed

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:606
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

She blossomed in perfect Beauty
To embody God.

She blossomed in perfect Duty
To reveal God.

She blossomed in perfect Immortality
To manifest God.

#+END_VERSE


* 607. Fate

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:607
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Human fate,
I am afraid of you.
Divine fate,
I am fond of you.
Human fate,
You remind me
Of the things I cannot do,
Which are far beyond my capacity.
Divine fate,
You tell me
That nothing is beyond my capacity,
Absolutely nothing,
For I am of God-Height
And
For God-Depth.

#+END_VERSE


* 608. Earth's glance, Heaven's glance

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:608
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Earth's hurtful glance
Has tortured me,
My body,
My life,
My all.
Alas, I know not
When and how or even why
Heaven's soulful glance
Will liberate me from my ignorance-body-life
And manifest me
In my wisdom-soul-life.

#+END_VERSE


* 609. It is high time

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:609
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Hope, sleep no more;
You have slept for a long time.
It is high time for you
To open your eyes.

Doubt, work no more;
You have worked for a long time.
It is high time for you
To close your eyes.

#+END_VERSE


* 610. Why do you hide?

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:610
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

God, why do You hide?
"I hide because
You are afraid of My infinite Love-power.
I also hide because
I want you to use
Your Aspiration-light
And make Me supremely proud of you."

#+END_VERSE


* 611. Daughter, such a long delay

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:611
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

"Daughter, such a long delay.
How do you account for it?"
I am embarrassed, Father.
I was having a heart-to-heart talk
With ignorance-night.
"Ignorance-night?
God bless you,
Since I dare not bless you."

#+END_VERSE


* 612. Father, such a long delay

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:612
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Father, such a long delay.
How do You account for it?
May I know?
"Certainly you may, My daughter.
I am sorry and embarrassed to say
That for a long time I have been living
In My Justice-Room,
And
Not in my Compassion-Palace."

#+END_VERSE


* 613. Complaints against humanity

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:613
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

A poet's complaint:
He is not appreciated
By humanity.

A philosopher's complaint:
He is not understood
By humanity.

A seeker's complaint:
He is ignored
By humanity.

A lover's complaint:
He is criticised
By humanity.

#+END_VERSE


* 614. Because God needs you

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:614
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Because
You do not love God,
You are useless.

Because
You do not need God,
You are worse than useless.

Because
God loves you,
One day He will make you useful.

Because
God needs you,
One day He will make you more than useful.
And I tell you,
That golden day
Is fast approaching.

#+END_VERSE


* 615. I have two hearts

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:615
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Unlike others,
I have two hearts:
A hiding heart
And
A crying heart.
My hiding heart shall feed
My earth-curiosity.
My crying heart shall feed
My Heaven-necessity.

#+END_VERSE


* 616. When I wait for God

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:616
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

When I wait for God
He may delay and delay,
But finally He comes;
He at least comes.
But when I wait for man
He simply never comes,
And he never will.

#+END_VERSE


* 617. Renewal

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:617
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Heaven-smile
Knows
How to renew itself.
That's all.

Earth-cry
Knows
Not only how to renew itself,
But also how to renew God,
The Beloved Supreme.

#+END_VERSE


* 618. God's Heart

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:618
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

God's Heart
May be big for humanity,
But not for me.
I tell you why:
I have easily concealed it,
I can easily reveal it.
Something more
(This time I shall have to tell
You in a whispering voice):
I shall reveal
God's Heart to you
Only to perfect you,
Fulfil you.

#+END_VERSE


* 619. His own friend and enemy

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:619
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

When he failed to serve God,
When he failed to love God,
When he failed to meditate on God,
He was felled by his own
Earth-generous friend: doubt
And his own Heaven-treacherous enemy: doubt.
Alas, alas!

#+END_VERSE


* 620. Too weak

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:620
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Too weak to watch
God-Smile,
Too weak to feel
God-Love,
Too weak to receive
God-Compassion,
Too weak to achieve
Inner cry.
Yet
I proudly claim
I am of God
And
I am for God.

#+END_VERSE


* 621. I love you more

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:621
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Plato -- Aristotle had a mind,
And
You have a heart.
I tell you frankly and unreservedly:
I love your heart more
And
Always shall.

Socrates -- Tolstoy had a heart,
And
You have a soul.
I tell you sincerely and proudly:
I love your soul more
And
Always shall.

#+END_VERSE


* 622. Evolution

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem

  :cite-key: EB:622
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Moral evolution:
Body-discipline,
Vital-discipline,
Mind-discipline.

Spiritual evolution:
Full God-awareness,
Entire life-perfection,
Complete love-oneness.

#+END_VERSE


* 623. No backward life

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:623
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

No eyes to look backward!
Therefore
I am happy.

No feet to walk backward!
Therefore
I am happy.

No mind to think backward!
Therefore
I am happy.
My sweet Lord is happy, too.

#+END_VERSE

Its purity-flood;

Its sincerity-flood;
And
My beloved Supreme has given me
His Compassion-filled
Necessity-flood.

#+END_VERSE


* 625. My flowers, my fruits

Of beauty
Are for Your Eyes.

Lord, my life-fruits
Of duty
Are for Your Feet.

#+END_VERSE

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:626
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

There was a time
When I was complete
In desire-life.

There was a time
When I was complete
In despair-life.

There was a time
When I was complete
In hope-life.

I am sure
There will be a time
When I shall be complete
Only in God-life.

#+END_VERSE

I see sun-beauty in her eyes.

In the evening
I see sun-peace in her eyes.

At night
I see sun-bliss in her eyes.

#+END_VERSE


* 628. Touch of life

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:628
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

O generous touch of sound-life,
I appreciate your concern
For me.

O precious touch of silence-life,
I admire your compassion
For me.

O gracious touch of oneness-life,
I love you,
I need you;
Eternally I shall love you,
Eternally I shall need you.

#+END_VERSE


* 629. Who has done this?

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:629
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Who has punctured his eyes?
Earth.
Sorry, not earth, but earth-doubt.

Who has polluted his ears?
Earth.
Sorry, not earth, but earth-jealousy.

Who has damaged his nose?
Earth.
Sorry, not earth, but earth-impurity.

Who has ruined his life?
Earth.
Sorry, not earth, but earth-ignorance.

#+END_VERSE


* 630. The champion of my new life

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:630
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Love-tree
Is the champion of my new life.
Devotion-flower
Is the champion of my new heart.
Surrender-fruit
Is the champion of my new soul.
With love-life I shall see,
With devotion-life I shall feel,
With surrender-life I shall become.

#+END_VERSE


* 631. My debts

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:631
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

My aspiration-realisation-life
Is my personal debt to earth.

My vision-delight-life
Is my personal debt to Heaven.

My progress-perfection-life
Is my personal
Plus
Eternal debt to God.

#+END_VERSE


* 632. I laugh and laugh

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:632
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

I laugh and laugh
When you spend time on hope.
I laugh and laugh
When he spends time on despair.
I laugh and laugh
When I spend time on destruction.
I laugh and laugh,
I laugh and laugh,
When God spends time on perfection,
Especially my perfection.

#+END_VERSE

  :PROPERTIES:

A set of rules.

Heaven-soul needs
No rules at all.

God-lover has only one rule:
God comes first.

#+END_VERSE

#+END_VERSE

Shall employ me.

#+END_VERSE

I am allowed
To sleep in the Heart of God;
Also,
I am allowed
To claim and proclaim God.

Realisation
I need to proclaim God.

Perfection
I need to become another God.

#+END_VERSE

The blue-white-gold
Banner of love,
I am vast,
I am divine,
I am perfect.

#+END_VERSE

With a delicious tongue.
Therefore
The greedy world needs me.

#+END_VERSE

My Heaven-capacity compels me

My earth-incapacity compels me
To be of no help to them.

#+END_VERSE

#+END_VERSE


* 651. Two languages

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:651
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

From Heaven's dreaming life
I learn the language of smiles.
I must say, it is a very difficult language.
Therefore
Everybody is afraid of it.

From earth's sleeping life
I learn the language of tears.
I must say, it is a very easy language.
Therefore
Everybody loves it.

#+END_VERSE


* 652. The torch of love

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:652
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

God made me
The torch of silence
To feed His celestial Height.

God is making me
The torch of life
To feed His terrestrial Space.

God shall make me
The torch of love
To feed His Heaven-beauty,
To feed His earth-duty.

#+END_VERSE


* 653. She

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:653
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Is her body.

Sun-duty
Is her life.

God-necessity
Is her heart.

#+END_VERSE


* 654. What are you doing?

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:654
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

"What are you doing?"
I am looking for a new path.
"I have one."
May I walk along your path?
"Certainly you may,
But first you must offer me
Your soulful cry."
Ah, you can have it immediately.

"What are you doing?"
I am looking for a new Master.
"I am the one."
May I have you as my Master?
"Certainly you may,
But first you must offer me
Your soulful smile."
Alas, it may take a little time,
But I shall definitely give it to you.

#+END_VERSE


* 655. High sunrise, low sunset

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:655
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

God-Compassion
Showed me my soul's
High sunrise,
Secretly and divinely.

World-examination
Shows me my life's
Low sunset,
Openly and deliberately.

#+END_VERSE


* 656. The superman

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:656
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

You are the superman of meditation.
Therefore
God loves you.
God loves you because you are great.

He is the superman of action.
Therefore
God loves him.
God loves him because he is good.

I am the superman of frustration.
Therefore
God loves me.
God loves me because I am helpless.

#+END_VERSE

Implanted in me.

* 661. My breathless necessity

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:661
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

God's Height
I have measured
Successfully and gloriously.

My two tiny feet
I fail to measure.
Why?
Just because I feed
Only the hunger
Of my breathless necessity.

#+END_VERSE


* 662. Out of sheer consideration

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:662
  :END:

God has transformed
My earth-tears
Into
My Heaven-smiles.

I shall convert
God-Dream
Into
God-Reality.
I promise I shall.

#+END_VERSE


* 663. Why do you blame me?

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:663
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Truth, I did look you up
Inside my mind.
But you were absent.
Now, why do you blame me unnecessarily?

Light, I did look you up
Inside my heart.
But you were absent.
Now, why do you blame me mercilessly?

Bliss, I did look you up
Inside my soul.
But you were absent.
Now, why do you blame me ceaselessly?

#+END_VERSE


* 664. Treasure and prefer

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:664
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

My dream-boat treasures.
Earth's terrestrial steadiness
My reality-shore prefers.

And I treasure
God's Compassion-height,
And I prefer
God's Forgiveness-light.

#+END_VERSE


* 665. The lover in him

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:665
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

The philosopher in him knows
All about Heaven-capacity
And
Earth-possibility,
But does not know
What is inside his heart-room.

The poet in him can tell you
All about God,
But he can never correctly tell you
Where God is.

The lover in him does not want to know
Who God is
And
Where God is;
It is enough for him
That God really /is/.

#+END_VERSE


* 666. My celebration

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:666
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

The same Compassion-God
Whom I saw before my birth-cry.
Yesterday I celebrated
God's Promise-day in me.

Today I see
This same Compassion-God
Inside the heart of my death-cry.
Today I celebrate
God's Hope-life in me.

#+END_VERSE

Give to all something.

I am happy

Because my heart is above fear.
I am happy
Because my soul is above bondage.
I am happy
Because my God is above ignorance.

#+END_VERSE

* 676. When this life dies

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:676
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

If you think
That this life immediately flies to God

You are wrong
If you think
That God comes down and immediately
Visits this life
When it dies.

You are right
If you feel
That this life gains an experience
Of God-Light
In the heart of God-Universality
When it dies.

* 678. Who believes?

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:678
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Who believes
In his God-life?
Nobody!

Who believes
In his God-realisation?
Nobody!

Who believes
In his God-realising aspiration?
Nobody!

Indeed, this is fate.
Needless to say
God's Pride is for him,
For him alone.

#+END_VERSE


* 679. The Himalayan ignorance-crest

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:679
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

If you aspire and then die,
Your life enjoys purposeful rest.

If you desire and then die,
Your life becomes a purposeless rest.

If you desire only to live
An animal life
Or
A human life,
Then you are living
On the Himalayan ignorance-crest.

#+END_VERSE


* 680. A God-sound

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:680
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

No joy in a slow sound,
No joy in a quick sound,
No joy in a low sound,
No joy in a big sound;
Joy only in a God-sound.
What is a God-sound?
A God-sound is my silence-life.

#+END_VERSE


* 681. Four inseparable friends

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:681
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

He lives in the room
Of brooding doubts.

She lives in the room
Of strangling jealousies.

You live in the room
Of devouring depression.

I live in the room
Of sighing lamentation.

Therefore
We are four inseparable friends.

#+END_VERSE


* 682. It can be better

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:682
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

I admire
The beauty of your eyes.
But it can be better.

I admire
The purity of your heart.
But it can be better.

I admire
The God-necessity in your life.
But it can be better.

#+END_VERSE


* 683. I feel really sorry for you

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:683
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Your heart-purity is snared
By the ignorance-world.
I feel really sorry for you.

Your mind-clarity is ridiculed
By the ignorance-world.
I feel really sorry for you.

Your vital-temerity is despised
By the ignorance-world.
I feel really sorry for you.

Your body-humility is misunderstood
By the ignorance-world.
I feel really sorry for you.

#+END_VERSE


* 684. God is all gratitude

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:684
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

God gave me a receptive life.
Therefore
I am all gratitude to him.

I gave God a deceptive smile.
Yet
God is all gratitude to me.
He says
At least I have given Him something.
There are countless souls on earth
Who have given Him
And will give Him
Nothing.

#+END_VERSE


* 685. Your golden today

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:685
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Don't be a liar!
Your yesterday was never golden.

Don't be a fool!
Your tomorrow can never be golden.

Be sincere, be wise!
Your today is unmistakably
And supremely golden.

#+END_VERSE


* 686. The plunge

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:686
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

My body-reality
Has plunged in man's
Fruitless sound-prosperity.

My soul-reality
Has plunged in God's
Fruitful Silence-divinity.

#+END_VERSE


* 687. My heart is enough

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:687
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

I have no need
For a sweet tongue.
My heart is enough.

I have no need
For a brilliant mind.
My heart is enough.

I have no need
For two strong arms.
My heart is enough.

I have no need
For two seeing eyes.
My heart is enough.

#+END_VERSE


* 688. Weeping

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:688
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Yesterday I wept
Because
I was not realised.

Today I weep
Because
I have not yet manifested God.

Tomorrow I shall weep
Because
I shall have failed to fulfil my
God-ordained tasks.

#+END_VERSE


* 689. I am caught

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:689
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

I am caught by an animal.
Therefore
I am ruthlessly commanded to surrender.

I am caught by man.
Therefore
I am unconditionally forced to offer.

I am caught by God.
Therefore
I am lovingly asked to love.
Why?
Because God wants me to become another God.
Why?
Because He wants me to be
His main partner
In His cosmic Game.

#+END_VERSE


* 690. Too proud

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:690
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

He was too proud to die,
He was too proud to live.
God said to him:
"Since you do not want to die,
You may as well
Work for me on earth.
Since you do not want to live,
You may as well
Sleep all day and night."

#+END_VERSE


* 691. The saga of my prayer

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:691
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

The saga of my prayer:
My prayer secretly comes down
From God-Compassion
And openly enters into the field
Of God-Manifestation.
Then,
My morning prayer is for earth-aspiration,
My midday prayer is for Heaven-satisfaction
And
My evening prayer is for world-perfection.

#+END_VERSE


* 692. No disguise

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:692
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

No disguise;
I love You.
My heart loves You only.

No disguise;
I need You.
My life needs You only.

No disguise;
You and You alone:
My Eternity's all,
My sweet beloved Supreme!

#+END_VERSE


* 693. Open house

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:693
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

My heart keeps
Constant open house.
Truth-duty every morning comes for breakfast,
Joy-beauty every noon comes for luncheon,
Light-divinity every evening comes for dinner.
My heart keeps
Constant open house.

#+END_VERSE


* 694. Three suns

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:694
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

The outer sun shines bright
At the end of my morning prayer.

My inner sun conquers my ignorance
At the end of my morning meditation.

My God-sun embraces me
At the end of my morning service.

#+END_VERSE


* 695. Chaos grows thick

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:695
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Chaos grows thick
As my body snores.

Chaos grows thicker
As my vital roars.

Chaos grows thickest
As my mind doubts.

Chaos grows thicker than the thickest
As my heart shouts.

#+END_VERSE


* 696. In the painted world

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:696
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

In the painted world
Who wants to live
Indefinitely?
Not I, at least!

In the painted world
Who does not want to play
The role of a saviour?
Needless to say,
I volunteer myself to be
The first saviour.

#+END_VERSE


* 697. Supreme command, supreme prayer

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:697
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

O my mind's doubt-life,
Leave me immediately.
Indeed,
This is my supreme command.

O my heart's faith-life,
O my life's surrender-light,
Guide me, guide me.
Indeed,
This is my supreme prayer.

#+END_VERSE


* 698. Human and divine

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:698
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Human life dies,
Divine life flies.
Human soul sees,
Divine soul becomes.
Human goal fails,
Divine goal succeeds,
Proceeds
And
Transcends.

#+END_VERSE


* 699. Every perfection-moment

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:699
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Every dedication-moment of mine
Adds a new lustre-soul
To God-Beauty.

Every perfection-moment of mine
Adds a new divinity-life
To God-necessity.

#+END_VERSE


* 700. The darlings

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:700
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Two are the darlings of Heaven:
Light and Delight.
Two are the darlings of earth:
Cry and Surrender.
Two are the darlings of God:
You and I.
But you must never breathe
This secret supreme to anyone.

#+END_VERSE


* Part VIII -- Poems 701 to 800[fn:: EB 701-800. Poems 701 to 800 were written in Stockholm and Uppsala, Sweden.]

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: section
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:701e1
  :END:



* 701. I maintain perfect freedom

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:701
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

I maintain perfect freedom
In my prayer.
I pray only to my Lord Supreme.

I maintain perfect freedom
In my meditation.
I meditate only on my Liberator Supreme.

I maintain perfect freedom
In my love.
I love only my Beloved Supreme.

#+END_VERSE


* 702. To deny their existence

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:702
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Do you want to deny
The existence of death?
Then start loving the heart of light.

Do you want to deny
The existence of Satan?
Then start becoming another God.

#+END_VERSE


* 703. A seat for death

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:703
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

In my soul-room
There is no seat for death.
In my heart-room
There is a seat for death.
But very often my heart
Does not allow death
To occupy its seat.
And what does my mind do?
My mind just welcomes death
And offers him any seat he desires.

#+END_VERSE


* 704. What matters?

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:704
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

What matters if I stand alone
And challenge the pride of falsehood?
Nothing!

What matters if I stand alone
And drink deep earth-poison?
Nothing!

What matters if I stand alone
And wait for God's Hour?
Nothing, absolutely nothing!

#+END_VERSE


* 705. Four divine servants

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:705
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Simplicity
Washes his body.

Sincerity
Cleanses his heart.

Purity
Purifies his breath.

Duty
Immortalises his life.

#+END_VERSE


* 706. How can I?

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:706
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

How can I teach the world
When it is so ignorant?

How can I feed the world
When it is not hungry?

How can I love the world
When it treasures ignorance?

#+END_VERSE


* 707. Paths to God

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:707
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

What is Life divine
If not a straight path to God?

What is Light divine
If not a sunlit path to God?

What is Love divine
If not a straight, sunlit shortcut,
A supreme shortcut
To God?

#+END_VERSE


* 708. Partners

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:708
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Who are you?
You are God's silent partner.

Who is he?
He is God's active partner.

Who am I?
I am God's sleeping partner.

Who is God?
A Reality-fulfilling Dreamer.

#+END_VERSE


* 709. Three visions of Christ

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:709
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

In his Humility
I saw Father Joseph's little son.

In his Compassion
I saw Mother Mary's big son.

In his Perfection
I saw his Heaven-Father's Smile.

#+END_VERSE


* 710. He loves his dreams

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:710
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

He loves his dreams
Because
They are thriving.

He loves his realities
Because
They are crying.

He loves his God
Because
He is always transcending.

#+END_VERSE


* 711. Desires unfulfilled

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:711
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Desires unfulfilled,
He dared to fling defiance at God.

Desires unfulfilled,
He trained himself in the denial of God.

Desires unfulfilled,
He at once became
God-indifference
And
Man-indifference.

#+END_VERSE


* 712. Alone with the Master

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:712
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

When you are alone with your Master,
You are not happy.
You feel sad that nobody is there
To appreciate you,
To admire you,
To consider you exceptional.

When you are in a group with your Master,
You are not happy.
You feel sad that you have to share
Your Master's presence with others,
His smile with others.
You are one of the many,
And in no way exceptional.

#+END_VERSE


* 713. Your inner sun

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:713
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Earth has allures,
Earth has mirages.
Be careful.
Are you looking for your
Own safeguard against
The aggression of your vital,
The suspicion of your mind,
The disintegration of your heart?
Then invoke your inner sun.
Your inner sun will offer you
Its clear shining.
It will, without fail,
Immortalise you.

#+END_VERSE


* 714. Your unflinching adherence

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:714
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

You want to embody me,
You want to reveal me,
You want to manifest me.
But how will you do all that?
By your unflinching adherence
To truth-silence,
To love-oneness.

#+END_VERSE


* 715. I shall do it for you

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:715
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Daughter,
You do not have to think;
I shall do the thinking for you.
You do not have to pray;
I shall do the praying for you.
You do not have to meditate;
I shall do the meditating for you.
You do not have to surrender;
I shall do the surrendering for you.
I shall do everything for you.
Just give Me a smile,
A soulful smile every day.

#+END_VERSE


* 716. Your Heaven

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:716
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Daughter,
Your Heaven is on earth.
Your Heaven is not a song-life,
Your Heaven is not a dance-life.
Your Heaven is your heart's oneness-life with Me.
Your Heaven is in your acceptance
Of God-light from Me.
Your Heaven is your real 'I'
In Me.

#+END_VERSE


* 717. Where our danger lies

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:717
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Where does your danger lie?
Your danger lies in your self-importance.

Where does his danger lie?
His danger lies in his pleasure-indulgence.

Where does my danger lie?
My danger lies in my world-rejection.

#+END_VERSE


* 718. Whom to blame?

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:718
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Why do you blame your circumstances?
Why do you blame others?
Why do you blame God?
You can blame and criticise
Only one person,
And indeed,
That person is you,
The ignorance-feeding
Dissatisfaction in you.

#+END_VERSE


* 719. You fail to claim God

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:719
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

You have seen God.
Therefore
You want to see God again.

You have loved God.
Therefore
You want to love God again.

You have surrendered to God.
Therefore
You want to surrender to God again.

But you have not done one thing:
You have not claimed God.
Therefore
You fail to claim God now.
Try to claim God;
Lo, God is proclaiming you.

#+END_VERSE


* 720. What you need

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:720
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

You do not need the trophy
Of your life-victory.

You do not need the appreciation
Of your life-story.

You do not need the recognition
Of your earth-bravery.

What you constantly need
Is your soul-flower.
What you breathlessly need
Is your heart-fragrance.

#+END_VERSE


* 721. In your case, in my case

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:721
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Twice my sincerity
Unreservedly speaks:
In your case,
It has taken you countless years
To learn some spiritual truths.
In my case,
Not some, but all spiritual truths
Come in a flash of glorious revelation.
You may verify this with God.
I do not mind at all.

#+END_VERSE


* 722. Easy lessons

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:722
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

When we deny God,
When we betray God,
He teaches us no easy lesson.
When we love God,
When we serve God,
He teaches us all easy lessons.
How?
Just by making all lessons easy,
Including even
Our God-realisation lesson.

#+END_VERSE


* 723. God is listening

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:723
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

God is listening;
Just speak quietly.
God is listening;
Just speak devotedly.
Believe me,
God is not and cannot be deaf
To your heart-longing.
His Compassion-perfection
Has caught the very first faint cry
From your oneness-heart.
God is listening;
Just speak quietly and devotedly.

#+END_VERSE


* 724. We are happy

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:724
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

You are happy
Because
You share with God
All the happenings,
Little and big,
In your life.

He is happy
Because
He loves God
Untiringly and unconditionally.

I am happy
Because
I have a real need for God.

#+END_VERSE


* 725. My supreme life

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:725
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

I pray and God grants:
Indeed, this is my human life.

I am of God and I am for God:
Indeed, this is my divine life.

I have and God is:
Indeed, this is my supreme life.

#+END_VERSE


* 726. The immediate assurance

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:726
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

I have seen the heart-tears
Of my sorrow-flooded life.
I also know that
Light-flooded God-Life
Is awaiting me --
The immediate assurance
Of my acceptance of God-Love.

#+END_VERSE


* 727. A truly willing guest

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:727
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

When my Lord Supreme
Is a truly willing guest,
He brings with Him His matchless treasure:
Compassion to me, His host.

When I am a truly willing guest,
I carry with me my long-forgotten treasure,
In fact, my only treasure:
Gratitude to God, my Host.

#+END_VERSE


* 728. He came to God

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:728
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

He came to God
With his business-filled days.
Yet
God-joy claimed him unreservedly.
God said: "Ah, My son has come at last."

He came to God
With his pleasure-filled nights.
Yet
God-joy claimed him immediately.
God said: "Ah, My long-lost son
Has come.
Today I am really complete."

#+END_VERSE


* 729. I knock, I plead, I cry

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:729
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

I knock
Because
My sweet Lord
Has once shown me His Heart-Door.

I plead
Because
My sweet Lord
Has once shown me His Soul-Room.

I cry
Because
My sweet Lord
Has once shown me His Silence-Throne.

#+END_VERSE


* 730. The link

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:730
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Father, I know who You are,
But I wish to hear it from You.
Do tell me who You are.
"Daughter, I am the link
Between
Your head and feet."

Father, I know who I am,
But I wish to hear it from You.
Do tell me who I am.
"Daughter, you are the link
Between
My Heaven-vision and Me,
My earth-mission and Me."

#+END_VERSE


* 731. My bosom-friends

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:731
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Varieties and separativities:
These are my bosom-friends
In my earth-existence.

Eternity and its trance,
Infinity and its smile,
Immortality and its life:
These are my bosom-friends
In my Heaven-existence.

#+END_VERSE


* 732. My partner

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:732
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

God, I need Your help only twice.
Please don't forget to help me.
When I live in ignorance-night
I wish You to remain with me
As my silent partner;
And when I want to leave ignorance-night
I wish You to be my
Active,
Dynamic
And
Victory-winning partner.

#+END_VERSE


* 733. Old story, new story

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:733
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

The story of my soul-sea
Is a very old story.
Therefore
My Lord Supreme does not want
To hear it anymore.

The story of my body-drop
Is absolutely a new story.
Therefore
My Lord Supreme is sleeplessly
Dying to hear it from me.

#+END_VERSE


* 734. God has dawned

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:734
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

God has dawned on my chaos-life;
Therefore,
From now on His cosmos
Shall remain perfection-light,
And my cry has found
A footpath to my world-peace,
My world-bliss.

#+END_VERSE


* 735. The Throne of God-Compassion

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:735
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

He sees the Throne of God-Truth.
Alas,
It is too high for him.

He sees the Throne of God-Light.
Alas,
It is too high for him.

He sees the Throne of God-Silence.
Alas,
It is too high for him.

He sees the Throne of God-Compassion.
Ah,
It is within his easy climb.
Lo, how unreservedly and perfectly he is enjoying
The blue-white
Throne of God-Compassion.

#+END_VERSE


* 736. Bewilderment

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:736
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

My soul is bewildered
When it sees my earth-ignorance.

My body is bewildered
When it sees my Heaven-plenitude.

My love of God is not bewildered
Even when it sees
The Infinitude of God.

#+END_VERSE


* 737. Immortal dawns, Immortal nights

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:737
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Immortal dawns
Of supreme excellence
I enjoyed with God in Heaven,
Unreservedly and unconditionally.
Alas,
Here on earth
Ignorance-sea has forced me to enjoy
Immortal nights
Of perpetual destruction-death.
O Compassion-Lord Supreme
Where are You,
Where am I?

#+END_VERSE


* 738. I weep

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:738
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

I weep for man's sake
Because
Man never learns,
Man never surrenders.

I weep for God's sake
Because
He has no other choice
Than to confide in me
The failure of His earth-promise.

#+END_VERSE


* 739. My earth is Heaven

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:739
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

My earth is Heaven
When my heart is all gratitude
To You, my beloved Lord Supreme.

My Heaven is earth
When I do not offer You,
My beloved Supreme,
My earth-transforming promise.

#+END_VERSE


* 740. If tomorrow fails me

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:740
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Yesterday failed me.
Therefore
My eye was on today.

Today is failing me.
Therefore
My eye is on tomorrow.

If tomorrow also fails me,
Like yesterday and today,
Then my eye shall be
On the Eternal Now.

Who is whispering?
Ah, my sweet Lord.
What is He whispering about?
He is offering me His Confidence-assurance.

#+END_VERSE


* 741. Why so cruel?

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:741
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Yesterday,
Why are you so cruel?
Why have you thrown yourself
Against my poor today?

Today,
Why are you so undivine?
Why are you throwing yourself
Against my poor tomorrow?

O human in me,
Why are you so stupid?
Why don't you throw yourself
Into God's eagerly awaiting
Compassion-Illumination-Sea?

#+END_VERSE


* 742. A high wall

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:742
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Man has raised a high wall
Between
Man and man.

God has built a solid bridge
Between
Man and God.

And I have established a powerful link
Between
My animal destruction
And my human frustration.

#+END_VERSE


* 743. Three immortal friends

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:743
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

On earth I have not one,
But three immortal friends:
Doubt, insecurity and despair.
In Heaven I have not one,
But three immortal friends:
Dream-boat, Confidence-soul, Promise-shore.

#+END_VERSE


* 744. The manager

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:744
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

He knelt.
Therefore
God blessed him.

He wept.
Therefore
God embraced him.

He prayed.
Therefore
God employed him.

He surrendered.
Therefore
God made him the manager
Of His cosmic Factory.

#+END_VERSE


* 745. His Heaven-palace

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:745
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Death struck
His earth-home
When he forgot to pray.
But God built
His Heaven-palace
With His Compassion-Ray.

#+END_VERSE


* 746. Two rarities

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:746
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

You are a Master
Rarer than radium.

I am a seeker
Rarer than radium.

God is the Forgiver
Of my blind folly
And
Your wild treachery.

#+END_VERSE


* 747. On Earth, in Heaven

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:747
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

On earth
I am a prisoner
Of animal wants
And
Human needs.

In Heaven
I am a darer
Of God-vision
And
God-satisfaction.

#+END_VERSE


* 748. My Heaven-smile

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:748
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

My Heaven-smile
Silenced my earth-cry
When it became too loud.

My earth-dedication
Fed my Heaven-dream
When it became too hungry.

#+END_VERSE


* 749. Our fate

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:749
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

You sail out to reach the shore
You are meant to reach.
He sails out to miss the shore
He is meant to miss.
I sail out to die;
I am meant to die.

#+END_VERSE


* 750. Because you cried yesterday

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:750
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Because
You cried yesterday,
Today you can smile.
Because
You are smiling today,
Tomorrow you, and nobody else,
Shall bring down
The Kingdom of Heaven
On earth
For God to enjoy His earth-rest
And man to enjoy his life-nourishing
Peace-nest.

#+END_VERSE


* 751. Into the life of perfection-love

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:751
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

My desire-life plunged
Into the life of destruction-sound.

My aspiration-life plunges
Into the life of satisfaction-silence.

My realisation-life shall plunge
Into the life of perfection-love.

#+END_VERSE


* 752. New creation, new creator

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:752
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

I don't want beauty,
I want power.

I don't want power,
I want love.

I don't want love,
I want light.

I don't want light,
I want God.

I don't want God,
I want a new creation
With the new creator: C.K.G.

#+END_VERSE


* 753. Because of you two

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:753
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Morality, you are too narrow,
Too limited.
Spirituality, you are too rigid,
Too strict.
Because of you two
My sweet beloved Supreme
Has become too compassionate,
Too indulgent.

#+END_VERSE


* 754. A more sincere student

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:754
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Although
God does not love me,
I love God.

Although
God does not need me,
I need God.

I am sure one day God will realise
His sad folly
And start loving me and needing me,
Perhaps as a more sincere student
Than I am.

#+END_VERSE


* 755. Loud questions, silent answers

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:755
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Earth's loud question:
Does God exist?

My loud question:
Is God alive?

Heaven's silent answer to earth:
God /does/ exist,
But
Not for you.

Heaven's silent answer to me:
God /is/ alive,
But
Not in you.

#+END_VERSE


* 756. The heart of tempting future

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:756
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

The animal in me tells me
How powerful I shall be.
The human in me tells me
How soulful I shall be.
The divine in me tells me
How fruitful I shall be.
Alas, I am doomed to live
In the heart of tempting future.

#+END_VERSE


* 757. Our two signatures

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:757
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Your signature embodies
Earth-aspiration.
My signature embodies
Heaven-compassion.
Don't think I am proud.
Only one thing
I want you to know:
If I don't dare to be sincere
To you,
Who else will and who else can?

#+END_VERSE


* 758. Claims

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:758
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Day-king claims my eyes
To be of service to him.
Night-queen claims my heart
To be of service to her.
I claim my life
To be of service to God-Dream
And
Man-transformation.

#+END_VERSE


* 759. Perpetual failure

  :PROPERTIES:
