  :cite-key: EB:759
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

I dream of nothing else
But a perpetual morning.

I see nothing else
But a perpetual evening.

I am nothing else
But a perpetual failure.

#+END_VERSE


* 760. The marathon of my fears

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:760
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Lord, my fears are tired.
They need some rest,
They deserve some rest.
I hope You agree with me
Totally.
If not, my fears shall continue
To run their endless marathon.

#+END_VERSE


* 761. One step ahead

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:761
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

My aspiration-dreams
Have cancelled
My desire-dreams.
Therefore
I am happy with my life
At long last.
My Lord Supreme
Is one step ahead.
Behold, He is mightily proud of me.

#+END_VERSE


* 762. Creation-power

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:762
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Man-power
Wants to create a new universe.

God-power
Wants to create a new man.

My power
Wants to create
A strict God
And
A perfect man.

#+END_VERSE


* 763. Before God's Feet

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:763
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Before God's kind Heart
I am half-stone.

Before God's strong Arms
I am half-animal.

Before God's clear Eye
I am half-human.

Before God's compassionate and forgiving Feet,
I must say, I am more than half-divine.

#+END_VERSE


* 764. Wings

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:764
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Satan claims to have
Imperious wings.

Heaven claims to have
Precious wings.

Earth claims to have
Generous wings.

God refuses to claim
His gracious Wings.

#+END_VERSE


* 765. I know, I know

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:765
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

I know, I know
He is the only ideal of my life.

I know, I know
He is the only thing real in my life.

I know, I know
His Compassion-smile
Is my Eternity's all.

#+END_VERSE


* 766. My armour

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:766
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

My faith in God
Was my yesterday's armour
Against world-temptation.

My patience in God
Is my today's armour
Against world-aggression.

My surrender to God
Shall be my tomorrow's armour
Against world-destruction.

#+END_VERSE


* 767. Be careful where you joke

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:767
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Be careful!
Don't joke at earth's gate.
Earth will bind you and blind you.

Be careful!
Don't joke at Heaven's gate.
Heaven may not accept you,
Heaven may not bless you.

Be careful!
Don't joke at God's Gate.
He may employ you to guard His Gate,
He may burden you with all
His endless responsibilities.

#+END_VERSE


* 768. Earth-time, Heaven-time

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:768
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

When earth-time sings,
I cry and cry.
I have failed, and no time is left.
When Heaven-time sings,
I cry and cry.
True, I have failed
And I am extremely tired,
But
Cruel Heaven-time
Neither discharges me
Nor grants me any rest.

#+END_VERSE


* 769. I have discovered

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:769
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Man's unconditional cry
I have felt.

God's unrevealed Smile
I have seen.

God's unmanifested Love
I have discovered.

#+END_VERSE


* 770. This time I shall not forget

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:770
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

This time I shall not forget
To ask my morning-brother to give me
His beautiful eyes as a gift.

This time I shall not forget
To ask my noon-father to give me
His powerful arms as a gift.

This time I shall not forget
To ask my evening-mother to give me
Her peaceful heart as a gift.

#+END_VERSE

  :PROPERTIES:

#+BEGIN_VERSE

Earth-sincerity meditates with me.
Therefore
I hope to see
One day
God's Face.

Earth-dedication meditates with me.
Therefore
I hope to be
One day
In God's Heart.

#+END_VERSE

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:773
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

His is the tongue
That cannot tell lies.

His is the life

His is the mind
That cannot deceive.

His is the heart
That cannot fail.

#+END_VERSE


* 774. The empty heart of night

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:774
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

When I am one
With the empty heart of night,
I offer her God's Heaven-light.

When I am one
With the heavy heart of night,
I offer her God's earth-sacrifice.

#+END_VERSE


* 775. His Eternity's goal-manifestation

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:775
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

HIS ETERNITY'S GOAL-MANIFESTATION

His Eternity's voyage-dedication
Is good.

His Eternity's pilgrim-realisation
Is better.

His Eternity's goal-manifestation
Is still unpredicted,
Nay, undecided.

#+END_VERSE


* 776. Our fate

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:776
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Slowly you glowed
But
Quickly you sank.
Alas, that is your fate.
Do you want to know
What my fate is?
I never glowed
And never shall.
I have been sinking and sinking.
Do you know when I stated sinking?
Long before the birth of Time.

#+END_VERSE


* 777. Heart and soul

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:777
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

The heart is better
Than the mind.
The mind knows it
But
It does not want to admit it.

The soul is better
Than the heart.
The heart knows it
And admits it.
Plus,
It takes great pride
In the sublime achievements
Of its ever-loving superior.

#+END_VERSE


* 778. An iota of will

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:778
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

I do not need
Factory-thoughts
To help me
In my self-discovery.
I need only
An iota of will
For my self-discovery,
God-victory
And
Earth-mastery.

#+END_VERSE


* 779. See if I am right

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:779
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Who says
Ignorance-life is
Beyond transformation?
Not true!
If you do not believe me,
Just enter into my past-room
And see if I am right.

Who says
God-discovery is
Beyond realisation?
Not true!
Just enter into my present-palace
And see if I am right.

#+END_VERSE


* 780. They shield my life

  :keywords:

#+BEGIN_VERSE

My God-faith shields my life
From despair-tornado.

My soul-faith shields my life
From doubt-clouds.

My heart-faith shields my life
From jealousy-frowns.

#+END_VERSE


* 781. His decay

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:781
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

He and doubt became good friends
His earth-aspiration decayed,
His Heaven-satisfaction decayed,
His God-compassion decayed,
His heart-perfection decayed.

#+END_VERSE


* 782. God-forgiveness

  :PROPERTIES:

#+BEGIN_VERSE

Ugliness is his inner life,
Deceitfulness is his outer life.
God-forgiveness transforms
His inner life
And
God-forgiveness perfects
His outer life.

#+END_VERSE

O proud body,
Be careful!
Ignorance-tiger is observing you.

#+END_VERSE

And
God's Immortality-descent
Together meet.

#+END_VERSE


* 785. Why to worship you

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:785
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Just because
You have realised God
I do not have to worship you.

Just because
You are revealing God
I do not have to worship you.

Just because
You are manifesting God
I do not have to worship you.

Just because
You love me more
Than I love myself
I shall worship you soulfully,
My heart shall worship you eternally,
My soul shall worship you unconditionally.

#+END_VERSE


* 786. Even while dying

  :PROPERTIES:

He was praying to Heaven
For world-transformation.

Even while dying
He was praying to earth
For earth-satisfaction.

Even while dying
He was praying to God
For death-illumination.

#+END_VERSE

* 789. My death is irreparable

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:789
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Your death is inconceivable.
Only Heaven is aware of it.
His death is incomparable.
Only death is aware of it.
My death is irreparable.
Friends, do not mind!
At times I allow my pride-horse
To play its usual role.

#+END_VERSE


* 790. Climb down, climb up

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:790
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Heaven climbed down
To measure his feet.
Earth climbed up
To measure her head.
I climb up to assist
Earth in her aspiration-flight.
I climb down to assist
Heaven in his dedication-dive.

#+END_VERSE

Made your mind a dark denier

Today

Tomorrow
Your soul shall make you grow
Into the ever-illumining God-Love.

#+END_VERSE

* 795. It is another thing to fall

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:795
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

It is one thing to love,
Another thing to fall.

Another thing to fall.
But
It is not two things
To escape and fall.

#+END_VERSE


* 796. The forgiver

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:796
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

God has not forgiven
My suspicious mind.
It is God's Indulgence
That has forgiven.

God has not forgiven
My ferocious vital.
It is God's Compassion
That has forgiven.

#+END_VERSE


* 797. My hunger

  :genre: poem

  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Yesterday
I was a power-hungry animal.

Today
I am a peace-hungry man.

Tomorrow
I shall become
A love-hungry God.

#+END_VERSE


* 798. He becomes a perfect God

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:798
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

When
He smiles,
He is a perfect Buddha.

When
He cries,
He is a perfect Ramakrishna.

When
He dances,
He is a perfect Krishna.

When
He prays,
He is a perfect Christ.

When
He meditates,
He no longer remains an Avatar;
He becomes another God,
A perfect God.

#+END_VERSE


* 799. Too much respect and love

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:799
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

You have too much respect
For the world.
I wish the world could give you
Something in return.

You have too much love
For the world.
I am sure God will crown
Your earth-dedication.

#+END_VERSE


* 800. You are armed

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:800
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

You are armed in mind-honesty.
You will go far.

You are armed in heart-purity.
You will go farther.

You are armed in soul-beauty.
You will go farthest.

You are armed in God-receptivity.
You will grow into the ever-transcending
Divinity's Reality.

#+END_VERSE


* Part IX -- Poems 801 to 900[fn:: EB 801-900. Poems 801 to 900 were written in Vasteras, Uppsala and Stockholm, Sweden and in Paris, France.]

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: section
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:801e1
  :END:



* 801. Life's younger brother

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:801
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

He was Life's younger brother.
Therefore
He was always given special attention
In the world of Life.

He was Death's elder brother.
Therefore
He had to take care
Of his younger brother.
This is the only reason
He used to spend so much time
With his younger brother, Death.

#+END_VERSE


* 802. My transformed life

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:802
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Imperfections can be transformed
Into perfect perfections.
Look, every morning
My transformed life
Prays to God
And
Meditates on God.
Every evening
My transformed life
Speaks about God
And
Serves God-food
To God-hungry souls.

#+END_VERSE


* 803. Old Master, new Master

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:803
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

At last he remembers
His old Master's name.
Justice-height
Is his old Master's name.
Alas he has forgotten
His new Master's name.
Compassion-light
Is his new Master's name.

#+END_VERSE


* 804. Your obedience

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:804
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

You fool,
Your obedience does not
Humiliate you.
Your obedience illumines you,
Your obedience takes you
To your own long-forgotten heights.
Your obedience
Is your earth-life's
And
Heaven-life's
Friend unparalleled.

#+END_VERSE


* 805. Unmistakably so

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:805
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Unbelievably but unmistakably,
I shall become another God.
Unmistakably yet unbelievably,
It is I who can
And will grant you realisation
After I have perfected
Your life within, without.

#+END_VERSE


* 806. Just wait and see

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:806
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Yesterday
I was the devouring desire of my animal life.
Today
I am the frustrated desire of my human life.
Tomorrow
I shall be a desire-liberated cosmic god.
Just wait and see,
Just see and wait
For your own hour.

#+END_VERSE


* 807. Enough!

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:807
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Hope, enough of your mockery!
Stop!

Doubt, enough of your treachery!
Stop!

Ignorance, enough of your bravery!
Stop!

Fate, enough of your slavery!
Stop!

#+END_VERSE


* 808. I do not doubt

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:808
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

I do not doubt man.
Why?
Am I a fool
To doubt my today's self?
No, I can't be that kind of fool.

I do not doubt God.
Why?
Am I a fool
To doubt my tomorrow's self?
No, I can't be that kind of fool.

#+END_VERSE


* 809. Always I am left behind

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:809
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Always
I am left behind
Because
I think too much.

Always
I am left behind
Because
I speak too much.

Always
I am left behind
Because
I love so little.

Always
I am left behind
Because
I serve so little.

#+END_VERSE


* 810. The eyes

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:810
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

The eyes of night
I was.
My vital life tempted the whole world.

The eyes of light
I am.
My heart-life is illumining the whole world.

The eyes of God
I shall be.
My Perfection-life shall immortalise the whole world.

#+END_VERSE


* 811. Roads

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:811
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Lord, the road to Heaven --
I must say,
My fear does not like it.
"I see."

Lord, the road to hell --
I must say,
My pride does not like it.
"I see."

Lord, the road to earth --
I must say,
My curiosity likes it.
Therefore
Here is my existence-light.
"I see."

#+END_VERSE


* 812. To make me happy

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:812
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

My soul
Embraces earth-essence
To make me happy.

My body
Embraces Heaven-essence
To make me happy.

My Saviour-God
Embraces earth-substance
To make me happy.

My beloved God
Embraces Heaven-substance
To make me happy.

#+END_VERSE


* 813. I do not blame him

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:813
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

His Compassion-wisdom failed.
Therefore
He left earth-reality
For Heaven-dream.
But I do not blame him.
Earth doubted
His Consciousness-light
Ruthlessly.
Earth challenged
His authority's divine authenticity
Sleeplessly.

#+END_VERSE


* 814. It really happened

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:814
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

It really happened:
God asked me to come down
And work for Him on earth.

It really happened:
I begged Him not to throw me
Into the Truth-devouring,
Light-devouring earth.

It really happened:
God told me that my service-light
Was badly needed for earth-transformation,
And that I was supremely chosen
By His own Height supreme.

#+END_VERSE


* 815. A common weakness

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:815
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

A common weakness:
To love ignorance.

A common weakness:
To doubt the existence of the soul.

A common weakness:
To forget God.

A common weakness:
To exaggerate Heaven-bliss.

A common weakness:
To ignore earth-beauty.

#+END_VERSE


* 816. When suspicion wakes

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:816
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

When
Aspiration wakes,
Suspicion sleeps.
When
Suspicion wakes,
Destruction jumps,
Life-beauty starves,
Heart-love dies.

#+END_VERSE


* 817. Out of sheer generosity

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:817
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Death, it is out of sheer generosity
And not out of necessity
That I give you my body.

Heaven, it is out of sheer generosity
And not out of necessity
That I give you my soul.

Earth, it is out of sheer God-necessity,
And my necessity too,
And not out of generosity
That I give you my God-achievements.

#+END_VERSE


* 818. Wishes

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:818
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

My soul's dear wish
Is to make my heart see
Heaven-light.

My heart's dear wish
Is to make my soul see
Earth-night,
Earth-cry,
Earth-tears.

#+END_VERSE


* 819. Daughter, you are

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:819
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Although I am finite,
Am I not Yours, Father?
"Daughter, you are."
Although I eat ignorance,
Am I not Yours, Father?
"Daughter, you are."
Although I forget to love You,
Am I not Yours, Father?
"Daughter, you are.
My daughter sweet, you are."

#+END_VERSE


* 820. I and death

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:820
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

My body saw death
Without fear.

My heart conquered death
With love.

My soul embraced death
With compassion.

I employ death
With no hesitation.

#+END_VERSE


* 821. From now on

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:821
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Heaven, for God's sake, do not accuse
My poor body any more.
My body
Is determined to aspire.
And I assure you,
It will aspire from now on.

Earth, for God's sake, do not accuse
My poor soul any more.
My soul
Is determined to reveal its light.
And I assure you,
It will reveal its light from now on.

#+END_VERSE


* 822. My life-beauty

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:822
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

My life-beauty knows no ignorance,
My heart-light knows no death,
My mind-peace knows no sound-life,
My vital-force knows no pleasure-life,
My body-surrender knows no sorrow.

#+END_VERSE


* 823. I run to death

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:823
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

I run to death
Because
Death loves my body,
If not my entire being.

Death runs to me
Because
I love death's silence,
If not its entire philosophy.

#+END_VERSE


* 824. The throne of hell

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:824
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

You do not have to go to hell
To see the throne of hell.
Just ask your suspicion-mind
To show you the throne of hell.
Your mind will not only show you,
But make you sit
On the throne of hell
With no charge at all.
Further, it will gladly allow you
To keep the throne
For your daily use.

#+END_VERSE


* 825. God's latest discovery

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:825
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

What is God's latest discovery?
Man? No!

What is God's latest discovery?
Man's aspiration? No!

What is God's latest discovery?
Man's dedication? No!

What is God's latest discovery?
Man's surrender? No!

What is God's latest discovery?
Man's gratitude-flames? Yes! Yes!

#+END_VERSE


* 826. Yet God loves me

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:826
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

I have all evil within me;
Yet God loves me.
Why?
Because He knows that my false modesty
Is not as bad as your God-denial.
Further, God knows that in my heart of hearts
I love Him dearly
And
Try to please Him unconditionally.

#+END_VERSE


* 827. Great years

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:827
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Heaven's great year is
1931.
Why?
Because in that year
I challenged earth-ignorance.

Earth's great year is
1944.
Why?
Because in that year
I discovered
Who I eternally am.

#+END_VERSE


* 828. First place

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:828
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Your God-love
Gets the first place in my heart.
Your God-service
Gets the first place in my mind.
Your God-manifestation
Gets the first place in my life.
You do not know,
Perhaps you will never know,
How proud I am always of you.

#+END_VERSE


* 829. The life that the Supreme lives

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:829
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

To me,
The life that the cosmic gods live
Is too monotonous.
Therefore
I do not care for it at all.

To me,
The life that the human beings live
Is too vociferous.
Therefore
I do not care for it either.

To me,
The life that the Supreme lives
Is most gracious.
Therefore
I sincerely care for it.

#+END_VERSE


* 830. My Lord's three faces

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:830
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

My Compassion-Lord
Is the eternal Forgiver.

My Love-Lord
Is the eternal Saviour.

My Peace-Lord
Is the eternal Comforter.

#+END_VERSE


* 831. A strange marriage

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:831
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

The son of ignorance:
Doubt.
The daughter of ignorance:
Jealousy.
They loved each other so dearly
That they got married.
Imagine, brother and sister
Getting married!
But it did happen.
They now have a son:
Destruction.

#+END_VERSE


* 832. Lord of my Heaven-life

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:832
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

O Lord of my Heaven-life,
Can I have You
As my own, very own?
"Amen!"

O Lord of my earth-life,
Will You have me
As Your own, very own?
"Amen!"

#+END_VERSE


* 833. Death's dateless night

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:833
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Death's dateless night
Is for him
Who knows how to cry
But
Forgets to try.

Life's dateless day
Is for him who does not try,
Just claims it.

Is this the correct thing to do?
My Lord says
It is absolutely correct.

#+END_VERSE


* 834. My life needs

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:834
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

My earth-life
Needs more beauty.

My Heaven-life
Needs more duty.

My realisation-life
For God-manifestation
Needs more of Heaven-soul
And
Earth-body.

#+END_VERSE


* 835. God is pleased

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:835
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Yesterday
I wrote good words.
God was pleased.
He shook hands with me.

Today
I am thinking good thoughts.
God is pleased.
He is blessing me.

Tomorrow
I shall do good things.
God will be pleased.
He will embrace me.

#+END_VERSE


* 836. My silence-life

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:836
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

My silence-life
Knows not how to boast.

My sound-life
Knows no modesty-coast.

My God-life
Knows no falsehood-host.

#+END_VERSE


* 837. Earth-mirror and Heaven-mirror

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:837
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

My thought-life whispers:
I will never see the Face of God.
My will-life thunders:
Who else is God,
Who else can be God if not me?
Is it not ridiculous to try
To see my own face?
I can easily see my face
At any time I want.
Earth-mirror and Heaven-mirror
Are always at my service.

#+END_VERSE


* 838. Today I am a little tired

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:838
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Be careful,
Arms of falsehood!
Tomorrow I shall challenge
Your power.
Today I am a little tired.

Be careful,
Eyes of ignorance!
Tomorrow I shall challenge
Your vision.
Today I am a little tired.

Be careful,
Head of Satan!
Tomorrow I shall challenge
Your brain.
Today I am a little tired.

#+END_VERSE


* 839. Favours

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:839
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Heaven,
I shall do you a favour.
I shall hide your deliberate indifference
Inside my mind-cave.
Now you do me a favour:
Place my heart-tears
Inside your eternally sailing
Dream-boat.

#+END_VERSE


* 840. Hesitation

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:840
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Where do I hesitate?
In my mind-room.
When do I hesitate?
The moment I shake hands
With falsehood.
Why do I hesitate?
I hesitate
Because
Still I have not claimed myself
As God's supremely chosen child.

#+END_VERSE


* 841. Who expects?

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:841
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Who expects my respect?
Only a fool.

Who expects my love?
Only a thief.

Who expects my concern?
Only a rogue.

Who expects my compassion?
Only a weakling.

#+END_VERSE


* 842. A reasonable God

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:842
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

You
Are a reasonable God.
Therefore
I eternally live inside
Your Dream-boat.

You
Are a reasonable man.
Therefore
I ceaselessly flow
With your hope-river.

#+END_VERSE


* 843. I am my own lover

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:843
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

In my body-life
I am my own destroyer.
In my vital-life
I am my own disaster.
In my mind-life
I am my own laughter.
In my heart-life
I am my own lover.

#+END_VERSE


* 844. Because of our sincerity

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:844
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Because
Of my necessity,
I love God.

Because
Of His Divinity,
God loves me.

Because
Of our sincerity,
We shall together
Forever stay.

#+END_VERSE


* 845. Goals

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:845
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

To be
God's sound-son
Was the goal of my outer life.

To be
God's silence-son
Was the goal of my inner life.

To be
God's surrender-son
Is the goal of my God-realisation-life.

#+END_VERSE


* 846. My present wisdom-light

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:846
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

I developed my first fear
By thinking that God did not care for me.
I developed my second fear
By thinking that God did not need me.
I developed my third and last fear
By thinking that God did not create me.

But now I know
How stupid I was.
And now I do something
Really significant and wise:
I do not allow my present wisdom-light
To mix with my ex-stupidity-night.

#+END_VERSE


* 847. Birthday observance

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:847
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Heaven's birthday I observe on earth,
Inside my silence-soul.

Earth's birthday I observe in Heaven,
Inside my vision-goal.

Heaven is one year younger than my beauty;
Earth is one year younger than my duty.

#+END_VERSE


* 848. All are lacking

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:848
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Doubt is something
That has no beauty.

Jealousy is something
That has no sanctity.

Insecurity is something
That has no unity.

#+END_VERSE


* 849. Forgiveness

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:849
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

God in me has forgiven
Heaven-intolerance,
Heaven-indifference.
But I
Cannot and shall not
Even try.
Never!


God in me has forgiven
Earth-aggressiveness,
Earth-possessiveness.
But I
Cannot and shall not
Even try.
Never!

#+END_VERSE


* 850. God's eternal Home

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:850
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Your heart
Is God's eternal Home.
Don't you see it?
Don't you feel it?
"No, I don't."
Alas, alas,
Then stay in my home, at least.
Don't get lost.
Stay in my house
Until I can take you
To God's Home, your real Home.

#+END_VERSE


* 851. Even my ignorance knows

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:851
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Why you love me
Is really far above
My earthly reasoning mind.

Why I need you
My heart-love knows,
My life-dedication knows,
Even my stupid ignorance blind knows.

#+END_VERSE


* 852. Too weak, too small

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:852
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Earth-love is too weak to receive
Heaven-strength.
Heaven-concern is too small to cover
Earth-length.

#+END_VERSE


* 853. Knowledge

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:853
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Desire was death.
I knew it,
I knew it painfully.

Aspiration is life.
I know it,
I know it cheerfully.

Realisation is oneness.
I shall know it,
I shall know it unmistakably.

#+END_VERSE


* 854. My Master I love

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:854
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

You are my Master of compassion.
Therefore
My heart loves you dearly.

You are my Master of realisation.
Therefore
My life loves you unreservedly.

You are my Master of perfection.
Therefore
I love you constantly
Plus
I need you immediately.

#+END_VERSE


* 855. They like to be

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:855
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

My mind
Likes to be cautious investigation.

My heart
Likes to be precious aspiration.

My life
Likes to be generous dedication.

#+END_VERSE


* 856. Death captures him

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:856
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Death loves him
Because
He is beautiful.

Death needs him
Because
He is powerful.

Death captures him
Because
He is not soulful.

#+END_VERSE


* 857. To live with you

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:857
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

O my doubt-life,
To live with you is to live
With mountains of misery.

O my faith-life,
To live with you is to live
With oceans of bravery.

O my aspiration-life,
To live with you is to live
In endless God-discovery.

#+END_VERSE


* 858. What my friends tell me

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:858
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

My conscience-friend tells me
What to do.

My consciousness-friend tells me
What to become.

My God-friend tells me
Who I eternally am:
Another perfect God.

#+END_VERSE


* 859. My sound-life

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:859
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

My sound-life
Gives me my world-hunger.

My silence-life
Gives me my world-peace.

My God-life
Gives me my world-satisfaction.

#+END_VERSE


* 860. Living by myself

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:860
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

There is joy even in death.
Why?
Because you and he
Will not accompany me.

There is joy even in hell,
Why?
Because you two will not be there.
I shall live by myself
Confidently and happily.

#+END_VERSE


* 861. Don't deny, don't forget

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:861
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Don't speak to him.
He is all evil.
Don't go near him.
He is all evil.

But don't deny
He, too, is of God.
But don't forget
He, too, is for God.

#+END_VERSE


* 862. They have forgotten me

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:862
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Heaven has forgotten me
Because
Heaven does not need my aspiration
Any more.

Earth has forgotten me
Because
Earth does not need my dedication
Any more.

Death has forgotten me
Because
Death does not need my ignorance
Any more.

#+END_VERSE


* 863. Past is past

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:863
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Past is past.
Also,
Past is dust.
He no longer likes his animal brutality.
He now loves divine reality
And
Unconditionally surrenders
To God's absolute Majesty.

#+END_VERSE


* 864. Lost and found

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:864
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Lost satisfaction-beauty found
At aspiration-door.

Lost perfection-lustre found
In surrender-cave.

The same way
Lost God will be found, too,
Somewhere, somehow,
Someday.

#+END_VERSE


* 865. The only answer

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:865
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

An austerity-life
Is not the answer
To my life-query.

An indulgence-life
Is not the answer
To my life-query.

An ego-surrendering life
With a God-loving heart
Is the only answer
To my life-query.

#+END_VERSE


* 866. Three Gods

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:866
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

The seeker in me
Is a baby God.

The worshipper in me
Is an adolescent God.

The lover in me
Is a fully mature God.

#+END_VERSE


* 867. Their strength

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:867
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Uncertainty!
Indeed, this is the strength of the mind.

Insecurity!
Indeed, this is the strength of the heart.

Impurity!
Indeed, this is the strength of the vital.

Absurdity!
Indeed, this is the strength of the body.

#+END_VERSE


* 868. Discoveries

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:868
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Desire-life has discovered:
"Light is dangerous.
It is always dogging me."

Aspiration-life has discovered:
"Ignorance-life is dangerous.
It is always chasing me."

Realisation-life has discovered:
"Nothing is dangerous.
Everything is struggling and striving
For its own existence."

#+END_VERSE


* 869. God alone knows

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:869
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

I wanted to become pure.
Therefore
My Master asked me to stop eating
Meat and fish.
I immediately stopped.
Alas, God alone knows
Where Purity-goddess is.

I wanted to become strong.
Therefore
My Master asked me to take
Regular exercise.
I immediately started.
Alas, God alone knows
Where Omnipotence-god is.

#+END_VERSE


* 870. The happiest person on earth

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:870
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Discipline your mind.
You will be happy.

Aspire from your heart.
You will be happier.

Surrender to God-light
What you have
And what you are.
You will be the happiest person on earth.

#+END_VERSE


* 871. The eye of the sun

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:871
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

The eye of the sky
Guides me, my fate.

The eye of the moon
Feeds me, my life.

The eye of the sun
Perfects me, my world.

#+END_VERSE


* 872. Let me sow

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:872
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Let me sow love
In my desire-life.

Let me sow joy
In my aspiration-life.

Let me sow perfection
In my realisation-life.

#+END_VERSE


* 873. God is tired

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:873
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

God is suddenly tired of Heaven.
Therefore
He is staying
Inside my heart-sky.

God is sincerely tired of earth.
Therefore
He is staying
Inside my soul-promise.

#+END_VERSE


* 874. Love she is

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:874
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Self-renouncing love
She has.
Therefore
We love her.

God-illumining love
She is.
Therefore
We need her, only her.

#+END_VERSE


* 875. Waiting

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:875
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

The eternal day of God
Waited for my God-realisation.

The eternal month of God
Waited for my God-revelation.

The eternal year of God
Shall wait for my God-manifestation.

#+END_VERSE


* 876. I don't have to worry

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:876
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

My soul thirsts for God-manifestation.
My heart thirsts for God-realisation.
My life thirsts for God-compassion.
I don't have to worry;
My soul has tremendous confidence.
I don't have to worry;
My heart has tremendous patience.
I don't have to worry;
My life has tremendous surrender.

#+END_VERSE


* 877. Love the lover

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:877
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Love the creator:
He is great.

Love the saviour:
He is good.

Love the lover:
He is indispersable.

#+END_VERSE


* 878. All are pleased

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:878
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

My life is pleasing everyone.
I please Heaven
With my heart-tears.
I please earth
With my soul-smile.
I please God
With my breathless life.
God, Heaven, earth:
I hope you three appreciate me.

#+END_VERSE


* 879. A life without

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:879
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

A life without soul-vision
Cannot succeed.
He knew it.

A life without God-aspiration
Cannot succeed.
He knows it.

#+END_VERSE


* 880. I do not stay with them

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:880
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

My soul is too indulgent.
Therefore
I do not stay with my soul.

My heart is too persistent.
Therefore
I do not stay with my heart.

My mind is too negligent.
Therefore
I do not stay with my mind.

My vital is too demanding.
Therefore
I do not stay with my vital.

My body is too unthinking.
Therefore
I do not stay with my body.

#+END_VERSE


* 881. Every existence

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:881
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Every existence says
Who it is,
Why it is.
Who is it?
God-dream.
Why is it?
Because it must feed God-necessity.

#+END_VERSE


* 882. The roar of mortal things

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:882
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

In him
I hear the roar
Of mortal things.

In him
I hear the snore
Of ephemeral life.

In him
I see the door
To perpetual hell.

#+END_VERSE


* 883. Today's heart-smilers

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:883
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Today's heart-smilers
Are
Tomorrow's light-lovers.

Tomorrow's light-lovers
Are
Day after tomorrow's
Ignorance-fighters.

#+END_VERSE


* 884. Why I love

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:884
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

I love death
Not because
Death loves me,
But because
Death needs me.

I love life
Not because
Life needs me,
But because
Life loves me.

#+END_VERSE


* 885. Freed from the devils

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:885
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Freed from doubt-devil,
I love Divinity.

Freed from jealousy-devil,
I love humanity.

Freed from hatred-devil,
I love Immortality.

#+END_VERSE


* 886. Honest promise, honest dream

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:886
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

My honest promise:
I shall please God
In God's own way.

My honest dream:
God shall need me
To found
His Divinity in earth-clay.

#+END_VERSE


* 887. God's Judgement-Seat

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:887
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

God's Judgement-Seat
Rules my Heaven-dreams.
God's Compassion-Feet
Feed my earth-realities.

#+END_VERSE


* 888. I shall give you

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:888
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Wait and see,
I shall give you
Earth-illumined dream.

Love and be,
I shall give you
Heaven-manifesting reality.

#+END_VERSE


* 889. Father, are you displeased?

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:889
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Father, are You displeased with Heaven?
"Yes, daughter, I am."
Why ?
"Because Heaven does not want to descend."

Father, are You displeased with earth?
"Yes, daughter, I am."
Why?
"Because earth does not want to ascend."

Father, are You displeased with me?
"Yes, daughter, I am."
Why?
"Because you do not want to consent."

#+END_VERSE


* 890. They tell me

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:890
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Light tells me
What I am.
Delight tells me
Where I came from.
Love tells me
Who I am.
God tells me
Whose I am.

#+END_VERSE


* 891. Perfect certainty

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:891
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Doubt-life
Is always
Worse than uncertainty.

Faith-life
Is at times
Black uncertainty.

Will-life
Expects certainty.

Surrender-life
Dances with perfect certainty.

#+END_VERSE


* 892. I am afraid of you

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:892
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

I am afraid of your pure greatness.
Therefore
I do not speak to you.

I am afraid of your sure frankness.
Therefore
I do not speak to you.

I am afraid of your complete God-oneness.
Therefore
I do not speak to you.

#+END_VERSE


* 893. Man's heart-smile

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:893
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Beauty is man's heart-smile.
Duty is God's Soul-smile.
Divinity is man's life-success.
Necessity is God's ever-transcending Progress.

#+END_VERSE


* 894. God knows how to cry

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:894
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

A fool knows how to boast.
I know how to challenge.
God knows how to cry
Pitifully.

A thief knows how to steal.
I know how to threaten.
God knows how to laugh
Roaringly.

#+END_VERSE


* 895. His freedom-choice

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:895
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Your choice is wrong!
You love your blind body.
Your freedom-choice binds you.
Ask God to choose for you.
He will choose your vision-soul.
His Freedom-choice will
Free you,
Fulfil you,
Immortalise you.

#+END_VERSE


* 896. Just a matter of time

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:896
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Lord, it is just a matter of time.
I shall bury
All my mind-curiosities.

Lord, it is just a matter of time.
I shall purify
All my heart-impurities.

Lord, it is just a matter of time.
I shall transform
All my life-imperfections
Into perfect perfection.

#+END_VERSE


* 897. The voice of night

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:897
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

The voice of night:
Temptation.
He knew it.

The choice of night:
Separation.
He knows it.

The noise of night:
Destruction.
He will know it.

#+END_VERSE


* 898. Beneath your soul's dignity

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:898
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

I have seen God.
You do not believe it,
You cannot believe it.
I tell you a supreme secret:
Your conduct is beneath
Your soul's dignity.
I have forgiven you.
But
I am afraid
Your soul will take some time
To forgive you.

#+END_VERSE


* 899. My inner wealth

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:899
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

What illumines my mind?
My inner faith.

What liberates my heart?
My inner sincerity.

What immortalises my life?
My inner cry.

#+END_VERSE


* 900. A noble thing

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:900
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Why has he decided
To love God?
Because his love has failed
Both Heaven and earth.

Why has he decided
To serve God?
Because his service has failed
Both Heaven and earth.

After all, it is a noble thing
To love and serve God.

#+END_VERSE


* Part X -- Poems 901 to 1,000[fn:: EB 901-1000. Poems 901 to 1,000 were written in Paris, France and in London, England and completed on July 13, 1974.]

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: section
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:901e1
  :END:



* 901. The mightiest God

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:901
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Justice-God
Is the mighty God.
My mind knew it.

Compassion-God
Is the mightier God.
My heart knows it.

Satisfaction-God
Is the mightiest God.
My life shall know it.

#+END_VERSE


* 902. I know who I am

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:902
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

The agelong veil is at last removed.
I now unmistakably know
Who I am.
I am a Truth-warrior,
I am a Light-seeker,
I am a God-lover,
I am a Nectar-enjoyer,
I am a Perfection-builder.

#+END_VERSE


* 903. I need them

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:903
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

O my morning sun,
You are beautiful, divinely beautiful;
Therefore
My earth-life needs you.

O my evening sun,
You are fruitful, supremely fruitful;
Therefore
My Heaven-life needs you.

#+END_VERSE


* 904. Realisation-peaks

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:904
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

My heart-boat plies
Between
Blind hopes and wild despairs.

My soul-bird flies
From
Realisation-peaks to revelation-valleys.

#+END_VERSE


* 905. One thing you cannot do

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:905
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

I love God.
You too can do that.

I speak to God.
You too can do that.

I reveal God.
You too can do that.

But I do one thing
Which you cannot do.
At every moment
I renew my unconditional surrender
To God's Compassion-light.

#+END_VERSE


* 906. A life untouched

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:906
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Two eyes untouched
By beauty I have.

One heart untouched
By love I have.

One mind untouched
By light I have.

One life untouched
By meditation-prayers I have.

#+END_VERSE


* 907. Gifts

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:907
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

My mind came to me
With a gift of doubt.

My heart came to me
With a gift of tears.

My life came to me
With a gift of despair.

God came to me
With a gift of Silence-smiles.

#+END_VERSE


* 908. Beauty-eyes

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:908
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

I love the beauty-eyes
Of Heaven-years
When I am sleeping and dreaming.

I love the duty-arms
Of earth-years
When I am struggling and striving.

#+END_VERSE


* 909. He is tired

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:909
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

His heart is tired
Of earth-tears;
Therefore
It cries for Heaven-smiles.

His soul is tired
Of Heaven-dreams;
Therefore
It longs for earth-realities.

He is tired
Of God-promises;
Therefore
He openly shuns God's company.

#+END_VERSE


* 910. When you go to visit

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:910
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

When you go to visit Heaven,
Be careful
Of its clever neighbour: hell.

When you go to visit death,
Be soulful.
You may be invited by its neighbour:
Immortality.

#+END_VERSE


* 911. The God-guide

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:911
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Father, father of mine,
Today I have come to you
With my sad failures
And
My lost opportunities.

"Daughter, daughter of mine,
Today you can claim me
To be your God-guide
To the Absolute Supreme,
Without tears
Without fears
Without frustration
Without hesitation."

#+END_VERSE


* 912. You are safe

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:912
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

You are safe
Amid earth-storms,
You are safe
Amid world-unrest,
You are safe
Amid life-insecurity,
Because
You do not want merely the truths
About God;
But you want God the eternal Truth
With His ceaseless and breathless Vision-Light.

#+END_VERSE


* 913. When you conquer temptation

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:913
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

When temptation
Conquers you,
Evil smiles at you
And evil smites you.

When you
Conquer temptation,
You become a channel
For God-power,
And God supremely treasures you.

#+END_VERSE


* 914. Talk to me, Lord!

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:914
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Talk to me, Lord!
You have not talked to me
For a long time.
What have I done?
Why are You so cross with me?
I am sorry to say
That You, too, act like
An ordinary human being.
You fail to maintain
Your fondness for one individual.
Your fondness consciously
Or aimlessly roams.
Am I right, my Lord?
Perhaps I am.

#+END_VERSE


* 915. I am always the same

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:915
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

I am always the same --
Yesterday, today, tomorrow.
But
Yesterday your aspiration-power told you
I am great.
Today your realisation-power tells you
I am good.
Tomorrow your perfection-power will tell you
I am constantly
Transcending
My greatness-height
And constantly
Increasing
My goodness-light.

#+END_VERSE


* 916. Each thought

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:916
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Each thought can be a golden opportunity.
Each thought can be a prayer.
Each thought can be a God-lover.
Each thought can be a man-transformer.
Each thought can be a world-liberator.
Each thought can be
An ever-transcending preparation
And
An ever-manifesting perfection.

#+END_VERSE


* 917. Possibility and impossibility

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:917
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

When I tell you
To give me your love,
I ask no impossibility.
You just give it.

When I tell you
To give me your devotion,
I ask no impossibility.
You just give it.

When I tell you
To give me your surrender,
I ask no impossibility.
You just give it.

But
When I ask you to give me
Your ignorance-night,
I ask an impossibility.
It seems you can never give it.

#+END_VERSE


* 918. Preludes

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:918
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Humiliation is a necessary prelude
To life-preparation.

Life-preparation is a necessary prelude
To love-manifestation.

Love-manifestation is a necessary prelude
To earth-perfection
And
God-satisfaction.

#+END_VERSE


* 919. Best and next best

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:919
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Aspiration-sun
Is the best thing in my earth-life.
Hope-moon
Is the next best thing.

Satisfaction-perfection
Is the best thing in my Heaven-life.
Dream-promise
Is the next best thing.

#+END_VERSE


* 920. Who is my friend?

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:920
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Who is my friend?
He whose heart is on active service.

Who is my friend?
He whose mind is above earth-fogs
And world-smokes.

Who is my friend?
He whose soul keeps my victory banner
Flying high, very high.

#+END_VERSE


* 921. Three examinations

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:921
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

I have passed
My first examination:
God-realisation.

I am passing
My second examination:
God-revelation.

I shall undoubtedly pass
My third examination:
God-manifestation.

#+END_VERSE


* 922. Are you a fool?

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:922
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Are you a fool?
Why do you starve
Your aspiration?
Aspiration is your future salvation,
Certain salvation.

Are you a fool?
Why do you feed
Your hesitation?
Hesitation is your future destruction,
Total destruction.

#+END_VERSE

#+BEGIN_VERSE

Yesterday
My name was God-preparation.

Today
My name is God-dedication.

Tomorrow
My name shall be God-satisfaction.

Indeed, these are the names
Of my life's adventure-saga.

#+END_VERSE

Depends
On your Heaven-recognition.

#+END_VERSE


* 927. Do not hesitate!

  :PROPERTIES:

  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:927
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Do not hesitate!
When you hesitate
You feel that the hour
Has not yet struck
For your God-revelation.
You are totally wrong.

Do not hesitate!
When you hesitate
You feel that God-manifestation
Is a far cry.
You are completely wrong.

Dive within and see the face of Truth.
When you hesitate
You delay God's Manifestation-journey.

#+END_VERSE

Why, why, Father?

You can and shall discover God
Once again.

  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:984

In spite of my best intention.

My Eternity's treasure
Unreservedly
And
Ceaselessly.

Is a minute of Duty's love.

#+END_VERSE


* 986. Love me more

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:986
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

You will understand me.

Another Lord Supreme.

#+END_VERSE


* 987. Tell others

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:987
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Tell others that I need them.
I shall need you more.

Tell others that I love them.
I shall love you more.

Tell others that I shall be
Proud of them eventually.
I shall be proud of you immediately.

#+END_VERSE


* 988. I shall never fail you

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:988
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

I shall never fail you.
Never!
My promise-flood depends not
Upon your aspiration-drop,
Or your perfection-grain.
It depends only on my own
Love-thirsty and
Oneness-hungry
Necessity.

#+END_VERSE


* 989. I shall not fail you

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:989
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Even
If you doubt me,
I shall not fail you.

Even
If you betray me,
I shall not fail you.

Even
If you deny me,
I shall not fail you.

But
I shall fail you
If ever you treasure self-pity.

#+END_VERSE


* 990. I shall use my God-Power

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:990
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Don't fling defiance at me!
I shall use my God-Power
To transform your ignorance-night
Into God-light.
I shall compel you
To be the distributor of
God-Height,
God-Depth
And
God-Nectar.

#+END_VERSE


* 991. The neighbour

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:991
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Your self-importance
Is a clear sign
Of your inner helplessness.

Your self-declaration
Is a clear sign
Of your inner emptiness.

But you are fortunate
Because
Your self-importance
And
Your self-declaration
Have
God-Compassion
As their immediate neighbour.

#+END_VERSE


* 992. No easy lesson

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:992
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

I teach no easy lesson;
I give no easy love;
I reveal no easy Light;
I am no easy Delight.

#+END_VERSE


* 993. Long before

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:993
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

I answered you
Long before you prayed.
But alas,
Your heart-receptivity
Was not functioning.

I loved you
Long before you received imagination-gift.
But alas,
Your oneness-necessity
Was not pressing.

#+END_VERSE


* 994. Let others serve you

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:994
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Let others share in your every gain.
Let others share in your every pain.
Let others love you
The way they want to.
Let others serve you
The way they want to.
You love them because you know
That their hearts are of your dream-boat,
And their lives are for your reality-shore.

#+END_VERSE


* 995. A God-man

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:995
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Not what you receive,
But what you give
Makes you a God-man.

Not what you conceive,
But what you achieve
Makes you a God-man.

Not how many times you try,
But how soulfully you cry
Makes you a God-man.

#+END_VERSE


* 996. I am fortunate

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:996
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

I am freely forgiven;
Therefore
I am fortunate.

I am secretly perfected;
Therefore
I am fortunate.

I am openly needed;
Therefore
I am fortunate.

I am unconditionally loved;
Therefore
I am fortunate, really fortunate.

#+END_VERSE


* 997. Your identity

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:997
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Who says
You are a weak mortal?
You are not!

Who says
You are an erring human child?
You are not!

What are you then?
You are God in His preparation
For His ever-transcending Height.

#+END_VERSE


* 998. To think of God

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:998
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

To think of God
Is to live in God's Kingdom.

To pray to God
Is to live in His Palace.

To meditate on God
Is to sit on His Throne.

To love God
Is to sing and dance in His Heart.

#+END_VERSE


* 999. This is how

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:999
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

Offer your heart-tears
To God.
This is how you must
Pray to God.

Offer your life-experiences
To God.
This is how you must
Meditate on God.

Offer your dream-goal
To God.
This is how you must
Love God.

#+END_VERSE


* 1000. Something sublime, something soulful, something fruitful

  :PROPERTIES:
  :genre: poem
  :keywords:
  :cite-key: EB:1000
  :END:


#+BEGIN_VERSE

You want to know something sublime
About my life?
My life is a God-dreamer.

You want to know something soulful
About my heart?
My heart is a God-lover.

You want to know something fruitful
About my soul?
My soul is a God-distributor.

#+END_VERSE
